## Why adam

adam is a **deterministic cognitive kernel for Kazakh** — rule-based dialog with auditable belief revision, morpheme-indexed retrieval, and a forward-chaining reasoner over typed facts, all running as a single tool-driven pipeline. It trades **generalisation for integrity**: every output is traceable, every belief revisable, every conclusion sourced. Every layer is **Rust-only** and **graph-first** by repository invariant — both enforced by contract tests.

### Architecture name — ARK (Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel)

**v4.55.5+** — adam's architecture is named **ARK** = Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel. Renamed from NLM (Nano Language Model) to mark adam's distinct architectural class: not a smaller LLM, but a different kind of system entirely. The four pillars:

- **A**gglutinative — Kazakh morphology decomposes deterministically (root + typed suffixes); composition is rule-bound, not learned.
- **R**easoning — a curated knowledge graph (`data/world_core/*.jsonl`) + a forward-chaining reasoner (10 active rules) produces every fact-bearing claim. Every output cites a source.
- **K**ernel — system-runtime, not a probabilistic estimator. ARK has small trained components (selection-weights perceptron, suffix-chain priors, root-affinity PMI) but they sit inside the kernel as inspectable layers, not at the centre.

Tiny ML lives, large ML doesn't: the trained perceptron is 24 bytes / 6 f32; suffix priors and root affinity are statistical but auditable. Generation is template-based, never free-text. Result: predictable, traceable, watch-battery-deployable Kazakh dialog.

### Engineering thesis

The project's core engineering claim — independent of any historical or philosophical thesis about Kazakh — is that **agglutinative morphology gives a clean algebra of meaning**: every Kazakh word decomposes into a root plus a sequence of typed suffixes, each contributing a known grammatical operator (case, number, tense, person, possessive, polarity, modality). Composition is rule-bound, not learned. That structure is exactly what we build the runtime on: FST morphology + typed suffix priors + root-pair PMI as deterministic prior layers, world_core as a curated graph of typed facts, and templates as the only path from fact to text. No probabilistic free generation. No retrained-from-scratch behaviour per release. The result is **predictable, traceable, low-energy** answer for Kazakh queries — not because the language has special metaphysical status, but because its structure is unusually friendly to formal modelling. The same engineering style would apply to other agglutinative-typology languages (Turkish, Kyrgyz, Tatar, Uzbek, …) without claims of universal grammar.

**v5.2.0 — Kazakh grapheme-to-phoneme (G2P) module — substrate for kernel-pure concatenative TTS.** First step toward fully-deterministic Kazakh pronunciation that doesn't depend on neural models or external TTS. New module [`adam_dialog::phoneme`](crates/adam-dialog/src/phoneme.rs) maps Kazakh Cyrillic text to a stream of [`Phoneme`] units via rule-based G2P. **Why bother:** Kazakh is heavily agglutinative with mostly-regular orthography — grapheme-to-phoneme is overwhelmingly 1:1 for the native 33-letter alphabet, with predictable handling of Russian-loan letters. Rule-based G2P fits `project_retrieval_not_neural_v2` philosophy and runs in microseconds. **Phoneme inventory:** 10 vowels (а ә е и ы і о ө ұ ү) + 23 consonants (б п м у ф т д н с з л р к қ г ғ х һ ш ж ч й ң) — 33 phonemes total. Russian-loan compounds decomposed: ё→j+o, ю→j+u, я→j+a, ц→t+s, щ→ʃ+tʃ. Hard / soft signs (ъ ь) silent. **API:** `Phoneme` enum + `text_to_phonemes(text) -> Vec<Phoneme>` + `phonemes_to_ipa(stream) -> String` for transcription debug + `Phoneme::is_vowel()` / `bank_id()` (ASCII-safe filename for future phoneme bank). **What's deferred to v5.2.5+:** the actual phoneme bank (audio WAV per phoneme) is a separate content-engineering investment requiring native-speaker recordings. v5.2.0 ships only the G2P module — useful in its own right for educational tools (phonemic transcription), phoneme-aware spell-checking, and future `PhonemeBankTtsBackend`. **Regression tests:** 20 new — vowel classification, IPA-symbol uniqueness, bank_id ASCII-safety, simple words («алма» / «құс» / «көйлек» / «таң» / «бағдарлама»), Russian-loan decomposition (ё / ю / я / ц / щ), hard/soft sign silent drop, whitespace/punctuation drop, uppercase normalisation, mixed Cyrillic+Latin, long-word stress test («бағдарламашылық»). **Verified:** workspace **1121 passing** (+20 from new v5.2.0 phoneme tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 5.2.0 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** the TTS arc (v5.0.0 + v5.0.5 + v5.1.0 + v5.2.0) builds toward **kernel-pure Kazakh voice** — a research direction nobody else is pursuing because OS-bundled or neural TTS are «good enough» for everyone except a project that explicitly wants offline-deterministic auditable pronunciation. v5.2.5+ phoneme-bank recording is the next frontier. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (kernel-pure pronunciation substrate).**

**v5.1.0 — Optional Piper neural TTS backend — richer voice for users who want it.** Adds a second `TtsBackend` implementation alongside the v5.0.0 OS-native default. Users who want noticeably more natural speech can install [Piper](https://github.com/rhasspy/piper) (~5 MB binary) and download a voice model (~50-100 MB ONNX), then run `adam_chat --tts --tts-backend piper --tts-model <path>`. **Architectural framing preserved:** Piper is bundled NEITHER in adam's binary NOR in the repo — it's purely opt-in, kernel determinism unchanged. **What's added:** new [`PiperTtsBackend`](crates/adam-dialog/src/tts.rs) struct backed by `piper` CLI + native audio player (`afplay` on macOS, `aplay` / `paplay` / `play` on Linux). `PiperTtsBackend::detect(model_path)` returns `None` if any of {piper binary, audio player, ONNX model file} is missing. Pipeline: `text → piper stdin → temp WAV → spawn audio player`. Audio player tracked in `Mutex<Option<Child>>` for the same kill-previous semantics as v5.0.5. **REPL flags:** `--tts-backend piper` opts in; `--tts-model <path>` points at the ONNX file. Graceful fallback to OS backend when Piper detection fails. **Helper functions:** `locate_command(name)` resolves a binary's absolute path via `which`; `locate_audio_player()` probes `afplay → aplay → paplay → play` candidates in order. **Regression tests:** 7 new — `piper_backend_describe_includes_model`, `piper_backend_accessors_work`, `piper_detect_returns_none_when_model_missing`, `piper_speak_empty_input_is_noop`, `locate_command_finds_known_binary_on_unix`, `locate_command_returns_none_for_missing_binary`, `locate_audio_player_finds_afplay_on_macos`. **Smoke test:** `adam_chat --once 'Сәлем.' --tts --tts-backend piper --tts-model /nonexistent.onnx` correctly logs «piper requested but not found; falling back to OS backend» and speaks via `say (voice: Aru)` — graceful fallback verified. **Verified:** workspace **1101 passing** (+7 from new v5.1.0 tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 5.1.0 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** for current macOS users, the bundled `Aru` voice (v5.0.0 OS backend) is already excellent — Piper backend is for Linux users without quality TTS, or anyone who wants experiment with different voice models. Kazakh-specific Piper models aren't in the official catalogue today, but the architecture is ready when one becomes available (or user trains one). **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (multi-backend voice infrastructure).**

**v5.0.5 — Non-blocking TTS dispatch — REPL stays responsive while adam speaks.** Builds on v5.0.0 voice output. Pre-v5.0.5 `OsTtsBackend::speak` blocked the REPL until the synthesiser finished — student could only type next input *after* adam stopped speaking. Post-v5.0.5 the synthesiser runs as a detached child process; speak returns in microseconds (spawn-and-forget) so the REPL accepts the next prompt immediately. **Latest-wins semantics:** if the student types a new query while a previous response is still being spoken, the previous synthesis is killed and the new one starts. Natural for interactive tutoring — old half-spoken responses don't queue up. **Touches:** [`tts.rs`](crates/adam-dialog/src/tts.rs) — `OsTtsBackend` gains a private `Mutex<Option<Child>>` field; `speak()` switches from `Command::status()` to `Command::spawn()`; `kill()` + `wait()` reap any previous child first. New `OsTtsBackend::new()` constructor + `program()` / `args()` / `voice()` accessors (former `pub` fields are now private with proper encapsulation). `Drop` impl best-effort reaps the last child on REPL exit (macOS `say` keeps speaking even after parent exits — the user hears the last response even after ^D). **Regression tests:** 3 new — `speak_returns_promptly_via_spawn_on_macos` (asserts elapsed < 250ms for a long sentence — would be ~5s if blocking), `second_speak_kills_previous_child_on_macos` (verifies kill-previous semantics by comparing child PIDs), `speak_empty_input_is_noop` (whitespace input doesn't spawn). **Verified:** workspace **1094 passing** (+3 from new v5.0.5 tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 5.0.5 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** with v5.0.5 the voice feature is finally usable for fast back-and-forth — student typing speed is no longer capped by adam's speaking rate. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (responsive multimodal output).**

**v5.0.0 — Voice output transducer — adam speaks Kazakh.** First multimodal release. Pre-v5.0.0 every adam response was silent text; post-v5.0.0 the optional `--tts` flag activates a system-native voice synthesiser so adam **speaks** every response in addition to printing it. **Architectural framing:** TTS is a **peripheral output transducer** — not a kernel component. The deterministic dialog kernel (intents, planner, realiser) produces the same Kazakh text as before; the TTS layer just speaks that text through the OS voice. Zero binary-size impact, zero new model dependency, kernel determinism preserved per `project_retrieval_not_neural_v2`. **What's added:** new module [`adam_dialog::tts`](crates/adam-dialog/src/tts.rs) with `TtsBackend` trait + `OsTtsBackend` (shells out to platform-native command) + `NoOpTts` (fallback). Detection prefers Kazakh voice (`Aru` on macOS, `kk` locale on Linux `espeak-ng`); falls back to default voice with one-time warning. `strip_for_speech` cleans markdown fences and inline backticks before synthesis (so `\`\`\`rust ...\`\`\`` doesn't pronounce «backtick backtick backtick rust...»). **REPL flags:** `--tts` activates voice output; `--tts-voice <name>` overrides voice detection. **End-to-end smoke test:** `adam_chat --once 'Сәлеметсіз бе.' --tts` produces «adam-chat: TTS on — say (voice: Aru)» and speaks the greeting through macOS Aru voice. **Regression tests:** 10 new module unit tests covering TtsBackend trait + NoOpTts + OsTtsBackend detection + voice override + `strip_for_speech` markdown handling. **Verified:** workspace **1091 passing** (+10 from new v5.0.0 tts tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 5.0.0 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** with v5.0.0 adam crosses from text-only to multimodal output — a kernel-signature step (warrants `x.0.0` per cadence policy). For Kazakh school deployment voice is a major UX upgrade: students hear correct pronunciation of grammatical concepts as they read code on screen. Roadmap (next): v5.0.5+ optional Piper TTS backend for richer voice; concatenative phoneme bank for fully-deterministic pronunciation; non-blocking dispatch for REPL responsiveness. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (multimodal output live).**

**v4.99.5 — Adaptive-difficulty wiring (long-term roadmap step 4).** Plugs the `StageProgress::difficulty_hint` API (added in v4.98.5) into actual content selection. Pre-v4.99.5 every student got the same canonical exercise per topic regardless of past performance; post-v4.99.5 the tutor scales: 2+ failures on a stage → **Easy** variant; 1+ clean passes → **Hard** variant; mixed/initial → **Normal** (canonical). **What's added:** new `pedagogical::exercise_for_with_hint(topic, hint) -> Option<&'static str>` returning a stage-tailored variant (or falling back to canonical `exercise_for(topic)` for Normal hint or unknown topics). Easy + Hard variants ship for all 5 canonical stages: `ownership` / `borrow` / `lifetime` / `traits` / `async` — 10 new curated exercises total, hand-tuned per difficulty. Conversation pre-stuffs `extra_slots["exercise_body"]` with the tailored body when `Intent::AskExercise(topic-in-curriculum)` fires; planner's `extra_slots` merge (v4.95.0 plumbing) overrides the canonical content from `extract_slots`. Diagnostic `extra_slots["difficulty_hint"]` slot exposes the chosen tier for `--trace` mode. **End-to-end smoke test:** real REPL — first AskExercise(ownership) → canonical (Normal); SubmitSolution(passed); next AskExercise(ownership) → Hard variant («Иелік пен функция тіркесімі. Мына кодты түзетіңіз: ...»). **Regression tests:** [`tests/curriculum_v4995_adaptive_difficulty.rs`](crates/adam-dialog/tests/curriculum_v4995_adaptive_difficulty.rs) — 9 new (Normal-falls-back, Easy/Hard differ from canonical, Easy ≠ Hard, unknown-topic-stays-None, non-curriculum-topic-ignores-hint, Kazakh-alias-«қарызға алу»-resolves, multi-turn `#[ignore]` end-to-end, synthetic 2-failures shifts to Easy). **Verified:** workspace **1081 passing** (+8 from new v4.99.5 tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.99.5 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** the tutor now genuinely adapts — struggling students see simpler exercises that build foundation; confident students see harder challenges that stretch them. Closes the long-term curriculum arc started v4.98.0. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (adaptive content selection live).**

**v4.99.0 — Student-side curriculum-query intents (long-term roadmap step 3).** Rounds out the lesson-state surface added in v4.98.0/v4.98.5: students can now **proactively ask** about their journey instead of only seeing celebratory pop-ups when stages auto-close. **Two new intents** (39 → **41**): `Intent::AskNextTopic` («Келесі қандай тақырыпты үйренсем?») and `Intent::AskCurrentProgress` («Менің прогресім қандай?»). **Detectors:** `detect_ask_next_topic` matches advance-marker × learn-marker × question-marker conjunction (handles «келесі / әрі қарай / кейін / енді» × «үйрен / тақырып / сабақ» × «? / қалай / не / қандай»); `detect_ask_current_progress` matches direct phrases («қай жерде тұрмын», «прогресім қандай», «қанша тақырып», «қай тақырыпты бітір», «жалпы қалай тұр», «қандай жетістік») plus compositional progress-noun + question-marker fallback. Both routed BEFORE pedagogical detectors so «келесі тақырыпты үйренсем?» doesn't trip AskExercise/AskPurpose. **Curriculum recap renderer:** new `Curriculum::render_progress_recap_kk(progress) -> String` produces multi-line Kazakh prose listing every stage's status (`✓ ... — бітті` for closed, `... — қазір` for current with prereqs met, `⊘ ... — құлыпта` for locked). **4 new template families:** `next_topic.suggestion` (3 variants) / `next_topic.complete` (2 variants for fully-completed curriculum); `current_progress.recap` (3 variants) / `current_progress.empty` (2 variants for fresh-state students with starter hint). **Conversation slot population:** AskNextTopic populates `next_stage_*` (or `__curriculum_complete__`); AskCurrentProgress pre-renders `progress_recap` (or `__progress_empty__` + first-stage label as starter). **End-to-end smoke test:** real 6-turn REPL — empty-state recap → AskExercise(ownership) → SubmitSolution(passed) → partial recap with mixed statuses → AskNextTopic still recommends ownership (1/2 — qazır). **Regression tests:** 3 new `Curriculum::render_progress_recap_kk` unit tests + 15 new in [`tests/curriculum_v4990_query_intents.rs`](crates/adam-dialog/tests/curriculum_v4990_query_intents.rs) covering detector positives/negatives + intent dispatch + template-family presence + slot references + 5 end-to-end multi-turn flows (empty / partial / closed-ownership advance / curriculum-complete celebration). **Verified:** workspace **1073 passing** (+18 from new v4.99.0 tests) + 16 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.99.0 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** with v4.99.0 the curriculum surface is symmetric — adam **announces** progress (v4.98.5) AND **answers** progress queries (v4.99.0). Tutor loop now feels guided in both directions. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (curriculum query symmetry).**

**v4.98.5 — User-facing auto-advance + adaptive-difficulty hooks (long-term roadmap step 2).** Builds on v4.98.0's curriculum tracking foundation. When a `passed` `SubmitSolution` verdict closes a curriculum stage, adam now auto-announces the achievement AND the next-step recommendation. **Plumbing:** `Conversation` pre-stuffs curriculum-closure context (`__stage_closes__`, `next_stage_label_kk`, `next_stage_summary_kk`, or `__curriculum_complete__`) into `extra_slots` before planning; the planner's `submit_solution.*` sub-key remap reads those slots and routes to one of two new families. **New template families:** `submit_solution.passed_stage_closed` (3 variants: «Жарайсыз! **Иелік** тақырыбы аяқталды (2/2). Енді **Қарыз алу** тақырыбына кіруге болады. {next_stage_summary_kk}»); `submit_solution.passed_curriculum_complete` (2 variants for the final-stage case where no next stage exists). **Adaptive-difficulty hook:** new `StageProgress::difficulty_hint() -> DifficultyHint::{Easy, Normal, Hard}` exposes a coarse signal (Easy when failed ≥ 2; Hard when 0 failures + ≥ 1 pass; Normal otherwise) — API surface only; content selection in `pedagogical::exercise_for_topic` will plug in for v4.99.0+. **End-to-end smoke test:** real REPL session — AskExercise(ownership) → clean snippet → standard `passed` (1/2) → AskExercise(ownership) → clean snippet → «Тамаша! Сіз **Иелік** тақырыбын меңгердіңіз (2 жаттығу шешіліп қойды). Келесі қадам — **Қарыз алу**: Иеленбей, тек қарызға алу...» (auto-advance fires). **Regression tests:** 4 new module unit tests (difficulty_hint thresholds) + 7 new integration tests in [`tests/curriculum_v4985_auto_advance.rs`](crates/adam-dialog/tests/curriculum_v4985_auto_advance.rs) (template-family presence + slot-references + 2 #[ignore] end-to-end with real `cargo check` covering ownership-closure and final-stage curriculum_complete paths). **Verified:** workspace **1055 passing** (+9 from new v4.98.5 tests) + 16 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.98.5 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** v4.98.5 makes the curriculum journey **visible** to the student — every closed stage triggers a celebration + roadmap nudge, so the tutor feels like a guide rather than a question-answering tool. v4.99.0 ships the student-side query intents (`AskNextTopic` / `AskCurrentProgress`). **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (curriculum auto-advance live).**

**v4.98.0 — Lesson-state curriculum tree (long-term roadmap step 1) — foundation for adaptive tutor progression.** First step of the long-term tutor arc beyond Codex's round-2 audit. Defines an ordered Rust pedagogical curriculum (`ownership` → `borrow` → `lifetime` → `traits` → `async`) externalised into [`data/dialog/curriculum/rust_progression.json`](data/dialog/curriculum/rust_progression.json) with prereq edges + per-stage `exercises_to_pass` gate. New [`adam_dialog::curriculum`](crates/adam-dialog/src/curriculum.rs) module exposes `Curriculum`, `Stage`, `StageProgress` types + `Curriculum::next_unlocked(progress)` for the "what's the recommended next step?" query. `Conversation::new()` autoloads the committed curriculum (silent `None` for trimmed checkouts); two new fields (`curriculum`, `curriculum_progress`) track per-conversation per-stage progress. After every `SubmitSolution` turn, `cargo_status` (`passed` / `failed`) increments the appropriate stage's counter — with two-tier topic resolution (planner-derived `topic` slot first, falling back to `session.last_exercise_topic` so an incidentally-extracted topic like `println` can't displace the lesson topic established by an earlier `AskExercise(ownership)`). v4.98.0 ships **only the tracking infrastructure** — user-facing response changes (auto-advance hint when a stage closes, recap templates) are deferred to v4.98.5; student-side query intents (`AskNextTopic` / `AskCurrentProgress`) to v4.99.0. **Regression tests:** 7 new `curriculum::tests` + 6 new `tests/curriculum_v4980.rs` (3 fast + 3 `#[ignore]` end-to-end with real `cargo check`) covering load + closure-threshold + next-unlocked + multi-turn pass-increment + fail-increment + non-curriculum-topic-no-pollution. **Verified:** workspace **1046 passing** (+10 from new curriculum tests) + 14 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.98.0 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** the tutor now has architectural memory of the student's curriculum journey — every successful exercise on a curriculum topic moves them measurably closer to the next stage. Adaptive difficulty (per-stage failure-rate signal) and proactive next-suggestion templates plug into this foundation in v4.98.5+. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (curriculum tree foundation).**

**v4.97.0 — Codex 2026-05-07 round-2 audit Bug 3 (P1) — REPL multi-line code-block accumulator.** Closes the last open Codex round-2 bug. Pre-fix: `adam_chat` read one line per turn, so a multi-line ` ```rust ... ``` ` block had to be entered with `\n` escapes — students couldn't paste real Rust source. Post-fix: when a line opens a fence that doesn't close on the same line, the REPL accumulates subsequent lines into a buffer until the closing fence appears, then submits the assembled block as a single turn input. Inline blocks (` ```rust X``` ` on one line — the v4.96.0 Bug 4 case) bypass the accumulator and process inline. Empty lines inside an open block are preserved (Rust functions can have blank separators); empty lines outside are skipped. **Touches:** [adam_chat.rs](crates/adam-dialog/src/bin/adam_chat.rs) — new `absorb_line(raw_line, &mut block_buf) -> Option<String>` state-machine helper + `count_fences(s) -> usize` parity counter. **Regression tests:** 10 new binary unit tests covering parity invariant + opening / body / closing sequence + inline-block bypass + empty-line behaviour. **Smoke test:** end-to-end multi-line Rust block via stdin → adam runs `cargo check` → returns «Жарайсыз!» verdict. **Verified:** workspace **1036 passing** (+10 from new REPL accumulator tests) + 11 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.97.0 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** with v4.97.0 the entire Codex 2026-05-07 round-2 audit (7 bugs total) is closed — bugs 1, 2, 4, 6, 7 in v4.96.0 + bug 5 in v4.96.5 + bug 3 in v4.97.0. Tutor REPL now accepts paste-friendly multi-line solutions out of the box. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (round-2 audit fully closed).**

**v4.96.5 — Codex 2026-05-07 round-2 audit Bug 5 (P1) — multi-turn anaphora resolves to pedagogical topic.** Fixes the gap where pedagogical intents (`AskExercise` / `CodeRequest` / `ExplainCompilerError` / `AskPurpose` / `CrossLanguageContrast` / `SubmitSolution`) emitted topic-bearing curated content but did **NOT** populate `Conversation.dialog_context`. Pre-fix scenario: «Маған ownership жаттығуын беріңізші.» → adam returns curated exercise → next turn «Оны қалай шешеміз?» — `dialog_context.resolve_anaphor()` returned `None` because only `Intent::Unknown` recorded topics. Post-fix: every topic-bearing pedagogical intent now writes `last_topic` + `subject_under_discussion` + `last_query_topic` so the existing v4.6.0/v4.13.0 anaphora resolver substitutes the lesson topic on subsequent turns. **Touches:** [conversation.rs](crates/adam-dialog/src/conversation.rs) — new match-arm extracts topic from all 6 pedagogical intent variants (incl. `CrossLanguageContrast.rust_concept`) and calls `dialog_context.record_turn` + populates `session["last_query_topic"]`. **Regression tests:** [`tests/codex_round2_v4965_anaphora.rs`](crates/adam-dialog/tests/codex_round2_v4965_anaphora.rs) — 8 new (per-intent recording + multi-turn resolution + topicless-no-pollution inverse). **Verified:** workspace **1026 passing** (+8 from new anaphora tests) + 11 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.96.5 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** with v4.96.5 the tutor lesson now survives anaphoric follow-ups within the same topic — student can ask «оны қалай түсіндіресіз?» / «бұл туралы тағы айтыңыз» without re-stating the topic each turn. Bug 3 (REPL multi-line accumulator) remains for v4.97.0. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor (multi-turn lesson coherence).**

**v4.95.5 — Multi-turn lesson state — adam links exercise prompt to next solution.** Closes the «учебное состояние ученика: тема → упражнение → ответ → диагностика → следующий шаг» gap from Codex's 2026-05-07 audit. When `AskExercise` (or `CodeRequest`) emits a topic-bearing prompt, adam writes `last_exercise_topic` to session. The next `SubmitSolution` turn — which typically arrives as a bare code block with no topic in prose — falls back to that stored topic and the verdict is framed in lesson context: «{topic} жаттығуыңызда **E0382** қатесі шықты — иә, бұл осы тұжырымдамада ең жиі ұрсу. ...». **Added:** `Conversation::absorb_entities` writes `last_exercise_topic` + `last_exercise_turn` when `Intent::AskExercise { topic: Some(_) }` or `Intent::CodeRequest { topic: Some(_) }` fires; planner falls back to session topic when `Intent::SubmitSolution { topic: None }`; lesson-aware variants in `submit_solution.passed` / `failed_known` / `failed_unknown` template families surface the topic; new `Conversation::session_value(key)` public read accessor for tests. **Integration tests:** 2 new `#[ignore]` tests verify multi-turn linkage — exercise→solution and code-request→solution. **Verified:** workspace **1008 passing** + 11 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.95.5 green; fmt + build clean. **Strategic:** with v4.95.5 the basic 4-turn tutor cycle works end-to-end — student picks topic, gets exercise, submits solution as code block, gets topic-aware verdict with E-code explanation. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor.**

**v4.90.0 — Rust Async Book chapter 4 deepening — Pinning (Pin + Unpin + self-referential structs).** Per-chapter pedagogical cadence continues. **v4.76.0 — `explain_steps` intent — narrate solution procedure.** Closes Codex round-2 Bug 2 family **fully** (3/3): solve_equation (v4.74.0) + check_answer (v4.75.5) + explain_steps (v4.76.0). After successful solve, user asks «Қалай шештің?» / «Процесін көрсет» / «Қадам-қадаммен түсіндір» → step-by-step narrative built deterministically by solver at solve time. **Innovations:** (1) Solver signature refactor: `try_solve_linear_equation` and `try_apply_formula` return `(unknown, value, steps)` 3-tuples. Step narratives in Kazakh: «Бастапқы теңдеу: x + 2 = 5. 2-ды екі жағынан да алып тастаймыз: x = 5 − 2 = 3» for linear; «Формула: F = m*a. Берілген: a = 3, m = 2. Орнына қою: F = 2*3 = 6» for formula. (2) New `try_explain_steps` detector (қалай шеш / процесін / қадам / түсіндір / дәлелде / шешуін көрсет). (3) Session storage: `last_math_steps` saved alongside `last_math_unknown` and `last_math_result`. (4) Conversation::turn post-pass: explain_steps runs AFTER math block (bare «Қалай шештің?» has no digits, math block doesn't fire). (5) New `explain_steps` template family (3 alternates). (6) Planner routes BEFORE check_answer/math_answer. **Verified:** linear/multiplication/formula explain narratives all surface correctly; check_answer + plain solves preserved. 100-query battery diff vs v4.75.5 = 0; 976 tests; clippy green. **Codex round-2 Bug 2 family complete (3/3).** Next: comparison shape (Bug 4, v4.76.5). **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor.**

**v4.75.5 — `check_answer` intent — verify user-submitted answer.** Closes Codex round-2 Bug 2 fully (verify-the-user's-answer half). Multi-turn pattern: solve equation → user submits «Жауабымды тексер: x=4» → system compares vs stored answer + responds correct/incorrect with explanation. **Innovations:** (1) new `try_check_answer` detector — pattern: check-phrase marker (тексер/дұрыс па/менің жауабым) + `var=N` token where var matches prior `last_unknown`. (2) Session-state extension: `last_math_unknown` stored alongside `last_math_result` after every solve. (3) Pre-check gate in math eval block — runs check_answer BEFORE arithmetic/linear/formula evaluators (prevents «x=3» being re-solved as trivial fresh equation). (4) Two new template families `check_answer.correct` / `check_answer.incorrect` in v1.toml. (5) Planner routes to check_answer.* family BEFORE math_answer when `__check_answer_correct__` slot present. **Verified flows:** «Егер x+2=5...» → «Жауабымды тексер: x=3» → ✅ «Дұрыс! x = 3»; same → «x=4» → ✅ «Жоқ, дұрыс жауап x = 3, ал сіз x = 4...»; «x=3 дұрыс па?» phrasing works; formula context («F=m*a, m=2, a=3» → «F=6 дұрыс па?») works. **First procedural capability requiring session state** — same pattern will apply to `explain_steps` (deferred). 100-query battery diff vs v4.75.0 = 0; 976 tests; clippy green. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor.**

**v4.75.0 — Paren-aware arithmetic — recursive-descent parser.** Replaces v4.74.x flat token-based evaluator with proper recursive-descent parser that respects parentheses and operator precedence. Closes v4.74.5 deferred «P=2*(a+b), a=5, b=3» honest-refusal case — now computes 16 correctly. **Innovations:** recursive-descent grammar (expr = term (('+'|'-') term)*; term = factor (('*'|'/') factor)*; factor = '-' factor | '+' factor | '(' expr ')' | number); arbitrarily nested parens; leading unary minus/plus; integer overflow via checked_* ops; division by zero → None. Kazakh-wrapper stripping from v4.74.0 preserved; kept-char set extended with `(` and `)`. Paren guard lifted in `try_apply_formula`. **Verified:** 2*(3+4) → 14, (5-2)*3 → 9, P=2*(a+b) (a=5, b=3) → 16, -10+(-5) → -15. All v4.74.x regressions preserved (5+7*2 → 19, x+2=5 → 3, F=m*a → 6, v=S/t → 5). Battery diff = 0; 976 tests; clippy green. **Deferred to v4.75.5:** `check_answer` intent (needs new template family + session state). Cadence: `.0` minor — entire arithmetic engine replaced. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor.**

**v4.74.5 — Procedural formula-applier — «F=m*a, m=2, a=3 болса F қанша?»** Second procedural solver in v4.74.x series. Closes Codex round-2 Bug 2 partial. **Innovations:** (1) new `try_apply_formula` parses comma-separated `var=expr` segments, categorizes one as formula (RHS contains alphabetic chars) and rest as numeric substitutions, then char-by-char substitutes single-letter variables and re-uses arithmetic eval. (2) Paren-rejection guard — current arithmetic evaluator doesn't respect parens, so formulas like «P=2*(a+b)» would silently mis-compute. Honest refusal beats wrong answer; will lift when paren-aware eval lands. (3) Try formula BEFORE linear-equation in Conversation::turn (formula inputs have multiple `=` tokens). **Verified:** F=m*a (m=2, a=3) → 6, v=S/t (S=100, t=20) → 5, S=a*b (a=4, b=6) → 24, P=2*(a+b) → honest refusal. 0 battery regression, 976 tests, clippy green. **Deferred:** paren-aware eval, check_answer intent, explain_steps intent, quadratic/multi-unknown solvers. Cadence: `.5` patch — additional solver in same architectural family. **Stripe — Kazakh school tutor.**

**v4.74.0 — First procedural solver — natural-Kazakh arithmetic wrapper + linear equation solver.** First step on the procedural-tutor roadmap. This release ships the simplest two solvers: arithmetic wrapped in natural Kazakh + 1-unknown linear equation. Both fully deterministic — no NN. **Bugs fixed:** «5+7*2 қанша?» → 19 (was refusal — cleaned string contained Cyrillic «қанша»); «Егер x+2=5 болса, x қанша?» → 3 (was refusal — no solver existed). **Innovations:** (1) `try_evaluate_arithmetic` pre-extracts longest contiguous arithmetic substring, dropping Kazakh wrapper words; (2) new `try_solve_linear_equation` — handles `x op a = b` and `a op x = b` for op ∈ {+, −, ×, ÷} with integer-solution gate; conservative — rejects multi-unknown, quadratic, fractional cases; (3) `Conversation::turn` integration via `__math_answer__` + `__math_unknown__` slot. **Verified:** 5+7*2 қанша = 19, x+2=5 → x=3, x*3=15 → x=5, 10-y=4 → y=6. **Acceptance:** 100-query battery diff vs v4.73.5 = 0 (no regression); workspace 976 passing; clippy `-D warnings` green; verify_release_version 4.74.0 green. **Deferred:** quadratic/multi-unknown solvers, formula-applier (`F=ma`), `check_answer` intent, `explain_steps` intent — scoped to v4.74.5+. **v4.73.5 — Codex round-2 bugs — factual-location routing fix + function-word topic blocklist + Earth-planet priority.** Driven by Codex 2026-05-06 round-2 review (after v4.73.0 ship). Codex confirmed v4.73.0 multi-turn fix worked, identified 8 additional failure patterns; this release fixes the 4 with surgical scope. **Bug 6 (critical):** «Қазақстанның астанасы қай қала?» → «Мен Қазақстан елімде» (false self-identity). **v4.55.5 — Architecture rename: NLM → ARK (Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel).** Driven by user decision (2026-05-05): the architecture name «NLM» (Nano Language Model) bucketed adam with the LLM family. **ARK** = Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel names what adam actually is — agglutinative morphology + curated knowledge graph + forward-chaining reasoner + tiny trained selection weights, packaged as a system-runtime not a probabilistic estimator. **Live REPL:** «Сен кімсің?» → "**ARK — Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel, мен адам атты қазақша тілдік модельмін.**"; «Танысайық.» → "**Иә, әрине. Мен — қазақша сөйлесуге арналған ARK, атым адам.**". **(1)** `SystemIdentity::canonical()` updated: `full_name = "Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel"`, `abbreviation = "ARK"`. **(2)** Latin-token whitelist in `quality.rs` extended with Agglutinative/Reasoning/Kernel/ARK; legacy tokens kept for historical compat. **(3)** Templates `greeting.intro_proposal` + `ask_about_system` updated to surface ARK. **(4)** 3 new world_core entries (`adam_self_040…042`): `adam IsA ARK` / `ARK IsA детерминирленген жүйе` / `ARK IsA архитектура атауы`. **(5)** 2 new MULTIWORD_ENTITIES (архитектура атауы, детерминирленген жүйе). **(6)** Eval data updated (cognitive_dialog_dataset.json, repl_dialogs.json, live_holdout_2026_05_01.json): assertions now accept ARK / Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel. **(7)** README — new «Architecture name — ARK» section documents the four-pillar definition + rationale; CONTRIBUTING.md Latin-whitelist bullet updated. **Naming history**: AGM rejected ("Grammar" school-feel), CALM rejected ("Controlled" tautological with "Agglutinative"), ARK accepted (Kernel = system-runtime; A+R+K each load-bearing). **Acceptance:** Workspace **976 passing** unchanged; foundation 2099/2359/46/28109 → **2102/2362/46/28112** (+3 entries / +3 facts / +3 derived from ARK identity facts); clippy `-D warnings` green; verify_release_version.sh 4.55.5 green; check_metrics_currency.sh green; fmt + build clean. **v4.53.5 — Context-aware clarify (session 5 generic-fallback complaint closed).** User's session-5 complaint: "ответы должны вытекать из контекста беседы, а не общий ответ на все, что не знает". When `Intent::Unknown` fires AND adam can't extract a noun-hint OR the topic is low-confidence, the v4.37.5 clarify path emitted a generic «Сұрағыңызды толық түсінбедім. Қандай тақырып туралы сұрап отырсыз?» — completely ignoring stored profile slots. v4.53.5 routes those clarify cases to a new `unknown.with_session_diagnostic` family that cites the stored context. **Live REPL replay:** vague follow-up after «Менің атым Дәулет, мен бағдарламашымын ...» → "**Дәулет, сізді бағдарламашы деп білемін. Сұрағыңыз мамандығыңызға қатысты ма, әлде басқа тақырыпта ма? Аздап нақтылаңызшы.**" (cites name + occupation; offers concrete topic choice). **(1)** New `unknown.with_session_diagnostic` template family with 7 variants gating on slot subsets (all 3 / name+occupation / name+activity / activity-only / occupation-only / city-only / name-only); `template_is_fillable` filters by actual session contents. **(2)** Planner override in `plan_response_with_epistemic` — runs AFTER the existing epistemic/known-user override block. When key is `unknown.clarify_no_topic` OR `unknown.clarify_low_confidence` AND session has any of name/occupation/activity/city, override to the new family. **v4.48.0 — Stage B bundle 7 — REPL-trace harvest substrate.** Pure-function trace-line parser. `HarvestReport` aggregates `selection_audit:` lines extracted from a batch of `Conversation::turn_with_trace` traces. `harvest_audit_traces(&[Vec<String>]) -> HarvestReport` walks each trace, counts audit lines + disagreements, preserves raw disagreement lines for hand-curation. **Pipeline:** Run Conversation programmatically → capture TurnTrace → pass to harvest_audit_traces → inspect disagreement_traces → hand-curate as new TrainingPairs → re-train via `train_perceptron` → ship as new `SelectionWeights::trained_v0`. **(1)** `HarvestReport { total_turns, multi_candidate_turns, audit_lines_found, disagreement_count, disagreement_traces }` + `disagreement_rate()` accessor. **(2)** `harvest_audit_traces` pure function (prefix-match `"selection_audit:"`; substring `"disagreement"`; preserves verbatim text). **(3)** Re-exports in `lib.rs`. **(4)** 7 new unit tests verify parser correctness (empty input, no-audit traces, disagreement preservation, agreement variant handling, multi-turn aggregation, multiple-lines-per-turn edge, prefix-vs-substring robustness). **(5)** Stage B substrate now complete end-to-end: every primitive needed to go from "raw REPL traces" to "trained, deployable weight table" exists as a typed public API. v4.48.5+ runs that pipeline on real data. **Verification:** Workspace **960 passing** (was 953; +7 new harvest tests); adam-dialog 293 passing (+7); selection module 48/48 (13 + 11 + 10 + 7 + 7); live REPL byte-identical to v4.47.5; foundation unchanged 2086/2346/46/27163; fmt + check clean. **v4.47.5 — Stage B bundle 6 — disagreement-case collection harness.** Pure-function aggregate substrate. `AuditAggregate` accumulates audit results across many gold pairs; `evaluate_weights_on_pairs(weights, pairs) -> AuditAggregate` runs the comparison for each pair and reports overall agreement / disagreement statistics + worst-case score gap. **v4.46.5 — Stage B bundle 4 — production trace-wiring (audit-only).** First production touch in the Stage B arc. v4.45.0–v4.46.0 built the substrate (foundation + training + canonical pairs + audit primitive) entirely off-path. v4.46.5 wires the audit primitive into the live `tool::search_graph` dispatch — when 2+ admissible candidates, run `selection::audit_compare` against the heuristic top-1 and push a trace line if the trained selector disagrees. **No behavioral change** — the heuristic still wins; the trace is read by `--trace` consumers to surface where the selector would diverge. **Architectural significance:** first time selection-weights infrastructure runs in production on real corpus facts. With `default_v0()` weights (hand-set to approximate v4.38.0 tiers), disagreement should be rare; each surfaced disagreement is a candidate for the v4.47.0+ training corpus. **(1)** Audit-only wiring in `tool::search_graph` — admissible-candidate guard + `audit_compare` call + trace push on disagreement (silent on agreement). **(2)** Trace-only architectural pattern (mirrors v4.42.0 NLG parallel-path). **(3)** `query_tokens` propagation reuses the v4.38.0 list-aware ranker's vec. **(4)** `last_topic` deferred to `None` (recency feature scores 0 for both candidates; tier collapses to no-op until v4.47.0+ ToolContext extension). **Verification:** Workspace **946 passing** unchanged; adam-dialog 279 passing; selection module 34/34; live REPL byte-identical to v4.46.0; foundation unchanged; fmt + check clean. Cadence: `.5` — first Stage B production-side touch + audit-only architectural pattern. **Stripe (11) — generative AI via agglutinative composition.**

**v4.46.0 — Stage B bundle 3 — canonical gold pairs + audit substrate.** Two architectural primitives connecting the v4.45.5 training algorithm to the future v4.46.5+ production wiring. **(1)** `canonical_training_pairs_v0()` — 15 hand-curated `(positive, negative)` gold pairs covering 5 feature dimensions (confidence axis × 3, subject-overlap × 3, object-overlap × 1, recency × 2, richness × 1, multi-signal interactions × 5) + the disambiguation scenarios that the v4.38.0 SearchGraph ranker tiers handle today. Pure deterministic constant. Train `default_v0()` on this set with `train_perceptron` and the resulting weights satisfy every canonical scenario by construction. **(2)** `AuditResult` struct + `audit_compare()` — pure-function side-by-side comparison of "what the heuristic ranker picked" vs "what the trained selector would pick" given the same candidate list. Returns `{ heuristic_top_idx, selector_top_idx, disagreement: bool, score_gap: f32 }`. Stable-tie-break matches `select_top` semantics. **(3)** Re-exports in `lib.rs`. **(4)** 10 new unit tests verify canonical-pair determinism / well-formedness / convergence / post-training rank correctness; audit agreement-vs-disagreement + score-gap reporting; degenerate-input handling. **(5)** No production wiring — pure infrastructure for v4.46.5+ trace integration. **Verification:** Workspace **946 passing** (was 936; +10 new audit tests); adam-dialog lib **279 passing** (+10); selection module 34/34 (13 + 11 + 10); canonical training pairs converge; live REPL byte-identical to v4.45.5; foundation unchanged 2086/2346/46/27163; fmt + check clean. Cadence: minor — Stage B bundle 3 (substrate for bundle 4 production routing + bundle 5 ranker replacement). **Stripe (11) — generative AI via agglutinative composition.**

**v4.45.5 — Stage B bundle 2 — pairwise margin-perceptron training pipeline.** Stage B continues. v4.45.0 shipped the foundation; v4.45.5 ships the training algorithm: pairwise margin perceptron that takes gold `(positive, negative)` candidate pairs and tunes `SelectionWeights` until every pair satisfies `score(positive) ≥ score(negative) + margin` (or `max_epochs` elapse). Pure function, deterministic per `(initial, pairs, config)`. **Architectural fit:** discrete (no gradient graph, no library deps), inspectable (still ~28 bytes after training), deterministic (no random sampling). Satisfies the thesis: «weights/learning OK if discrete, inspectable, cheap; reject only LLM internals». **(1)** `TrainingPair` struct (positive vs negative gold pair). **(2)** `TrainingConfig` with `learning_rate / margin / max_epochs` (default_v0: lr=0.1, margin=0.5, max_epochs=200). **(3)** `TrainingStats` reports `epochs_run / final_violations / converged`. **(4)** `train_perceptron(initial, pairs, config)` — the loop; per-epoch iterates pairs; failing pairs trigger update by `lr × (pos − neg)` per weight component; early-exit on zero violations. **(5)** Re-exports in `lib.rs`. **(6)** 11 new unit tests verify convergence on linearly-separable data, determinism, no-op when pre-converged, max-epoch reporting, empty-pair handling, single-dimension signal pickup (recency / confidence), zero-lr no-progress, multi-signal convergence, post-training rank correctness, stats reporting. **(7)** Not yet — real training data extraction from evals, audit-only wiring, production routing. **Verification:** Workspace **936 passing** (was 925; +11 training tests); adam-dialog lib **269 passing** (+11); selection module 24/24; live REPL byte-identical (no wiring yet); foundation unchanged 2086/2346/46/27163; fmt + check clean. Cadence: `.5` — 5 distinct innovations + kernel-signature algorithm. **Stripe (11) — generative AI via agglutinative composition.** Next: v4.46.0 — bundle 3 (real training data + audit-only wiring); v4.50.0 — trained-weights replacement of heuristic ranker.

**v4.45.0 — Stage B opens — selection weights foundation.** Stage B architectural milestone — first patch. The substrate for the project's stated path to LLM-comparable abilities without LLM costs. New `crates/adam-dialog/src/selection.rs` (~390 lines + 13 tests) defines tiny inspectable feature-weight tables that, in subsequent Stage B patches, will pick among rule-generated candidate responses. **Architectural significance:** Stage A built typed primitives + rule-based NLG + 46 curated domains; **Stage B starts here:** selection among candidates. Each weight is a single number in a table, readable by any human, deterministic per seed, no softmax sampling. **(1)** New `selection` module — `CandidateFeatures` (5 hand-extracted features: confidence / raw_text richness / subject overlap / object overlap / recency match), `SelectionWeights` (6 numbers + bias = ~28 bytes for v0), `extract_features`, `score`, `select_top` (stable-tie-break by first index for byte-identical regression). **(2)** Confidence mapping — `HumanApproved → 1.0` / `CuratedQuote → 0.8` / `RuleInferred → 0.5` / `RepeatedPattern → 0.3` / `Grammar → 0.0`. **(3)** Token overlap — query tokens (≥ 3 chars, casefold) matching the slot root. **(4)** 13 new unit tests (deterministic feature extraction + correct scoring + stable selection). **(5)** Re-exports in `lib.rs`. **(6)** Foundation-only — no production wiring (mirrors v4.42.0 NLG-foundation pattern). **Verification:** Workspace **925 passing** (was 912; +13 new selection tests); adam-dialog lib **258 passing** (was 245; +13); selection 13/13; live REPL byte-identical (no production wiring); fmt + check clean. Cadence: minor — Stage B opens (kernel-signature architectural arc). **Stripe (11) — generative AI via agglutinative composition.** Next: v4.45.5+ — training pipeline + first audit-only wiring; v4.46.0+ — production routing; v4.50.0 — trained weights replace heuristic ranker.

**v4.43.9 — `multiword_entity_hint` inflected-FIRST-word pass (architectural cleanup).** Closes the v4.43.8 architectural carry-forward. v4.43.8 fixed the «Қазіргі Қазақстан президенті» routing by registering both bare-form AND Gen-form variants of office phrases as multiwords — solved the symptom, but registering parallel Gen-form variants is data-drift waiting to happen. v4.43.9 lifts the fix to the matcher itself: a **third pass** in `multiword_entity_hint` detects inflected-FIRST-word forms via the six Kazakh genitive suffixes (-ның / -нің / -дың / -дің / -тың / -тің), so future 2-word multiword entries no longer need parallel Gen-form registration. Byte-identical for all v4.43.8 surfaces. **(1)** Third pass in `multiword_entity_hint` — for 2-word entities `X Y`, accepts input `X{Gen} T` where T starts with Y's first 3 chars and X{Gen} is X + one of the six Kazakh genitive suffixes. Conservative: parts[0] ≥ 4 chars. Returns BARE-form entity for SearchGraph canonical lookup. **(2)** 6 new unit tests (anti-regression on first/second pass + 4 new third-pass cases: bare-form return, voiceless «-тың», nasal «-ның», voiced «-дің», short-first-word skip gate). **(3)** Architectural cleanliness: future 2-word multiword additions can register bare-form only; matcher handles Gen-form input automatically. **Verification:** Workspace **912 passing** (was 906; +6 new matcher tests); adam-dialog lib **245 passing** (was 239; +6); multiword coverage green; live REPL replay byte-identical to v4.43.8 on president/premier queries; fmt + check clean. **v4.43.8 — v4.43.7 carry-forward closed: current-president direct routing.** Closes the v4.43.7 carry-forward where «Қазіргі Қазақстан президенті кім?» fell to abstract «Қазақстан президенттігі» (the office concept) instead of naming Тоқаев. Root cause: FST analyzes «президенті» as either `президент + Pos3` or `президенттік + Pos3`; the multiword «қазақстан президенттігі» wins via longest-substring match. Fix: 5 direct office-holder bridge facts + 5 multiword Gen-form / bare-form variants ensure topic-extraction picks the bridge-to-officeholder fact regardless of input surface. **Now:** «Қазіргі Қазақстан президенті кім?» → "**Қазіргі қазақстан президенті мен қасым-жомарт тоқаев өзара байланысты.**". «Қазақстанның президенті кім?» → links to Тоқаев. «Қазақстанның премьер-министрі кім?» → links to Бектенов. **All 6 v4.43.7-transcript gaps now materially closed (was 5/6).** **(1)** 5 direct office-holder bridge facts (gov_kz_016–021) in `government_kazakhstan.jsonl`. **(2)** `MULTIWORD_ENTITIES` += 5 for both bare-form and Gen-form (-ның) variants. **(3)** Foundation expansion — 2018 → **2019 entries**, 2277 → **2284 facts**, 26 854 → **26 869 derivations**. **Verification:** Workspace **906 passing** unchanged; adam-dialog 239 passing; multiword coverage green; live REPL 6/6 transcript-gap replay; fmt + check clean. **v4.42.0 — Stage A opens — rule-based NLG over typed semantic frames (foundation).** Opens **Stage A** of the project's refined thesis: adam as a NEW class of generative AI that uses the agglutinative paradigm — typed primitives + rule-based composition + tiny selection weights — to be safe / cheap / predictable while reaching LLM-comparable abilities. Templates were the rough draft; rule-based NLG over typed `SentenceFrame`s is the proper architecture. **(1)** New `crates/adam-dialog/src/nlg/` module with `render_sentence(frame) -> Option<String>` public API. **(2)** `SentenceFrame` typed wrapper — `{fact, mood, introducer}` mirrors agglutinative pattern (root + operators). **(3)** `NlgRule` trait — pluggable rule shape; trait-object polymorphism for community contributions. **(4)** 5 starter rules covering most-frequent factoid response patterns: IsA copula declarative («X — Y»), PartOf declarative, HasQuantity (reuses curated raw_text), RelatedTo list-summary, LivesIn declarative. **(5)** 7 unit tests covering each rule path + Direct/AboutTopicFirst/OnTheSubjectMain/BrieflyAbout introducer variants + unknown-predicate fallthrough. **(6)** In-flight regression fix: «Қазақстанның барлық аймақтарын тізімдеңіз» was returning notable-people list instead of облыстар list — `қаза`-prefix false-positive in direct_overlap; skip-list extended; синоним path correctly identifies облыстар. **Stage A status:** v4.42.0 lays the foundation; NLG runs as parallel path (templates unchanged); subsequent v4.42.x will migrate template families to rules; ~v4.50 opens **Stage B** (tiny selection weights). **Verification:** Workspace **884 passing** (+7 NLG tests); regression fixed; anti-regression on all controls; fmt clean. Foundation: 1819 entries / 1985 facts / 41 domains / 25 633 derivations. Cadence: minor — new module + new public API + opens multi-release architectural arc per versioning rule. **Stripe (10) → Stripe (11) — generative AI via agglutinative composition.** Next: v4.42.x — widen rule coverage (interrogative mood, more predicates); ~v4.50 — Stage B selection weights.

**v4.41.0 — Word-form math (Kazakh-language arithmetic) — 7-innovation bundle; coverage 85.28 % → 86.21 %.** First minor in v4.41+ arc. New kernel-signature capability: adam now understands and computes Kazakh-language arithmetic phrasings, returning both digit and word-form results. **Before:** «Бесті отызға көбейтсем» → "Санақ-есептеу әлі қазақша сөйлемдер арқылы менің мүмкіндігімде жоқ..." (refusal). **After:** "**Есептедім: 150 (жүз елу)**". User-explicit feature ask. **(1)** `try_evaluate_kazakh_word_math` evaluator — pipeline: detect math op via stem-prefix match (`көбейт*` / `бөл*` / `қос*` / `есепте*` + closed inflected-form set for `ал`-subtract); extract operand chunks using case-morphology as separator (Acc/Dat/Abl explicit case closes a chunk); compute integer; `None` on overflow / non-integer division. **(2)** Math-verb detection — switched to stem-prefix match catching all bare imperatives / converbs / conditionals; sentence-final-position rule for bare «ал» (math sense, distinct from sentence-initial conjunction). **(3)** Number-word parser — recognizes 0-9 / tens / 100 / 1000 / 10⁶ / 10⁹ in bare AND case-suffixed forms; composes compounds («жүз елу» = 150, «бір мың тоғыз жүз тоқсан тоғыз» = 1999, «екі мың» = 2000). **(4)** Case-morphology operand separator (compound numbers vs separate args). **(5)** `render_kazakh_number_words` — inverse renderer (0…999_999_999 → canonical Kazakh phrase) surfaced alongside digit via `__math_words__` slot. **(6)** Math template family extended with `{math_words}` slot. **(7)** Lexicon coverage batch — 7 new entries (облыс / республика / мақсат / спорт / видео / алғашқы / жатыр). Coverage **85.28 % → 86.21 %** (+0.93 pp). Cumulative v1.5.5 → v4.41.0: **79.48 % → 86.21 %** (+6.73 pp). **Verification:** Workspace **877 passing** (+12 from v4.39.7 baseline 865; 5 new word-math tests, 7 case-suffix synthesis tests); anti-regression on discourse anaphora preserved; foundation 1754 entries / 1920 facts / 39 domains / 25 501 derivations; fmt clean. **v4.39.7 — FST archiphoneme split + lexicon batch + segmenter disambiguation — 7-innovation patch bundle; coverage 83.27 % → 85.28 %.** Largest patch bundle since v4.6.5. Closes the v4.39.0 architecture-note carry-forward (FST `realise_d` gap on nasal/vowel-final case suffixes) AND lifts morpheme coverage by +2.01 pp via high-frequency lexicon batch. **(1)** New `{DN}` archiphoneme (Gen) and `{DA}` archiphoneme (Abl) — encode the «D-nasalization» rule as a forward-walking dispatch (Gen: nasal/vowel→н, default→д; Abl: nasal-only→н, vowel→д), distinct because Abl on vowel is `-дан/-ден` not `-нан/-нен`. ACCUSATIVE migrated to `{N}` archiphoneme. Vanilla `{D}` preserved for Loc/LocAttr. **(2)** 7 new synthesis-direction case tests (Gen on nasal/vowel/liquid/voiceless, Acc on nasal/vowel, Abl on nasal). **(3)** `genitive_topic_hint_for_list` simplified to parse-stream (was string-level workaround in v4.39.0; now uses FST-derived Genitive directly). **(4)** 11 high-frequency lexicon entries: бас / бет / мал / орта / орыс / пайда / қол / сөз / баста / отыр / орналас. **(5)** `deterministic_segment_parse` — fewest-segment-preference disambiguates root-collision ambiguity (frozen postpositions like «басқа» win over compositional «бас + қа»; truly compositional forms still segment normally). **(6)** Morpheme coverage **83.27 % → 85.28 %** (+2.01 pp); cumulative v1.5.5 baseline → v4.39.7: **79.48 % → 85.28 %** (+5.80 pp). **(7)** Bonus: «Адамның мақсаты не?» / «Сөз туралы» / «Бас деген не?» now correctly resolve to bridge facts. **Verification:** Workspace **872 passing** (+7 new case-suffix tests); 13 case-form roundtrip OK; bug 4 preserved via FST parse-stream; tokenizer 464/464 exact match; fmt clean. Pipeline: 2 new archiphonemes + 1 ACC migration + 7 tests + 1 hint simplification + 11 lexicon entries + 1 segmenter rule. **v4.38.5 — Lexicon pollution purge + FST P3+Acc derivation fix.** First patch in v4.38+ arc. Closes bug 4 carry-forward from v4.38.0 (lexicon registered «аймақтарын / аймақтары / аймақтар» as separate noun roots → FST never normalized inflected surfaces to bare «аймақ»). **Before:** «Қазақстанның барлық аймақтарын тізімдеңіз» → "Аймақтарын туралы нақтырақ не білгіңіз келеді." (clarify on mis-extracted topic). **After:** "**Аймақ туралы ең әуелі мынаны айтуға болады: Аймақ — аумақ.**" (correct root + bridge fact). **(1)** 85 inflectional duplicates purged (80 from `segmentation_roots.json` + 5 from `apertium_imported_roots.json`); strict suffix filter («-тарын / -терін / -ларын / -лерін / -дарын / -дерін» + shorter), base ≥ 4 chars to skip false positives like «қаңтары» → «қаң». **(2)** FST gap fix in `synthesise_noun`: when pronominal-н buffer is injected for P3+Accusative, the regular `ACCUSATIVE` template is now skipped — in Kazakh the pronominal-н IS the accusative marker after P3 («аймақтарын» = аймақ + Pl + P3 + н, NOT «аймақтарынды»). Other P3+case combinations (Dat/Loc/Abl) preserved. **(3)** Discovery: pollution masked the FST gap pre-v4.38.5; purge is a forcing function for FST coverage going forward. **(4)** All inflected forms now resolve to bare roots: «Аймақтарын / Тұлғаларын / Жазушыларын» → аймақ / тұлға / жазушы. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; bug 4 topic-extraction fixed; anti-regression on qty queries / confident facts / greetings; fmt clean. **v4.38.0 — Quantity-aware ranker + subject-synonym fallback + 53 role-bridge facts.** First minor in v4.38+ arc. Per `project_bridge_fact_leverage`: each bridge multiplies R1 transitivity output. Reasoner derivations 24k → **25 435** (+6 % from 53-fact addition). **(5)** `MULTIWORD_ENTITIES` += 8 compound bridge objects. **(6)** `LIST_TYPE_SYNONYMS` += бала↔ұл / қала↔мегаполис / ел↔мемлекет / кісі↔адам / тұлға↔адам. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; all 7 quantity classes (өзен/көл/тау/ұлттық саябақ/облыс/қала/ауыл) route correctly; anti-regression on type-list queries; foundation validation **1750 entries / 1916 facts** clean; fmt clean. **v4.37.5 — Human-like clarification on low-confidence topic extraction.** First behavioural release in v4.37+ arc. Closes a real-REPL pattern from the 2026-05-03 transcript: when topic extraction recovered only a fallback candidate (an adjective surfaced as `Analysis::Noun`, or a deverbal participle that registers as `noun` in the lexicon), the response asserted a tangential fact about that candidate confidently. Pre-fix the system either echoed the wrong word or cited a corpus quote about a modifier the user clearly meant as a qualifier. **Before:** «Қазақстанның атақты жазушыларын атаңыз» → "Атақты — атақ-атолу аффиксі..." (confident definition of an adjective). **After:** "Сіз атақты жайында сұрап отырсыз деп ұқтым. Дұрыс түсіндім бе? Толығырақ айтсаңыз болады." (clarify, invite correction). **(1)** New `TopicConfidence` enum on `Intent::Unknown.noun_hint_confidence` — fifth analytical signal (after polarity, modality, evidence, inversion-question). **(2)** Two-pass `first_noun_root_with_confidence` prefers `part_of_speech == "noun"` AND demotes deverbal participles ending in `-ған/-ген/-қан/-кен` (closes «шыққан» hijacking topic over «тұлға»). **(3)** Confidence-aware `best_noun_hint_with_confidence` threads the band through every extraction strategy. **(4)** Discourse-anaphora promotes confidence to High after substituting prior topic (preserves multi-turn anaphor list-class continuation). **(5)** Planner: `Low` confidence ALWAYS routes to `unknown.clarify_low_confidence` (even with retrieval evidence — corpus citation about an adjective is noise, not signal); `noun_hint == None` AND no_evidence → `unknown.clarify_no_topic` (replaces bare «Түсінбедім»). **(6)** Two new template families — `unknown.clarify_low_confidence` (5 templates) + `unknown.clarify_no_topic` (5 templates) — purely meta-conversational, surface inferred subject and hand the next turn back. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; live REPL bugs 2/3 fixed; gibberish now hedges; greetings/name/confident-fact controls unchanged; anaphor list-class continuation preserved; fmt clean; live latency 0.33 s / 176 MB (within v4.37.0 noise). **v4.37.0 — «X емес пе?» inversion-question routing — confirmation-seeking shape recognized.** First minor in v4.37+ semantic-IR arc. Closes v4.36.7 carry-forward. The «X емес пе?» pattern — tag-question form like «Бұл дұрыс емес пе?» («isn't this correct?») — is **not** a denial; it's a confirmation-seeking inversion where speaker EXPECTS X to be true. Pre-fix, v4.33.5 negation routing misread these as denials. v4.37.0 detects via «емес» + question-particle co-occurrence and routes to dedicated family. **Before:** «Бұл дұрыс емес пе?» → "Дұрыс емес деп айтасыз — пікіріңізді сыйлаймын." (denial misread). **After:** "Иә, мүмкін солай шығар — нақты дерегім жоқ." (inversion engagement). **(1)** New `Intent::Unknown.input_is_inversion_question: bool` field — fourth SemFrame-derived signal (after polarity, modality, evidence). **(2)** Conversation::turn detects «емес» (any inflected) + tag-question particle (бе/ма/ме/па/пе) co-occurrence. **(3)** Planner inversion routing — HIGHEST priority among Unknown-routing (before polarity). **(4)** Epistemic-override bypass mirrors prior pattern. **(5)** New template family `unknown.with_inversion_question` (7 templates) using hedging «мүмкін / шығар / ықтимал» — engages without confirmation or denial since adam lacks ground truth. **Battery case 18 reframed:** «Сен бағдарламашы емессің бе?» previously closed v4.34.0 as denial; v4.37.0 reroutes to inversion (semantically closer to intent). Battery `neg-consumed` 5/5 → 4/5 — **not a regression**, refinement; case 18 moved to inversion-consumed (script needs inv-consumed metric, deferred). **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; mean **195.3 ms / 176.1 MB** (+3.8 ms vs v4.36.7, within noise); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. Pipeline: 1 new Intent field + 2 propagations + 6 test patches + Conversation population + planner short-circuit + override bypass + 1 new template family. Cadence: minor — fourth SemFrame-derived dialog signal. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.37.5 (fourth matcher migration; battery inv-consumed metric); v4.38+ (RelationKind; remaining 6 parser tenses).

**v4.36.7 — EvidenceKind consumption on extraction side (Hearsay refuse) — Evidence cycle closed both sides.** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Closes substrate-then-consume cycle for **Evidence on extraction side** (mirroring v4.36.0's dialog-side). Adds third guard — Hearsay refusal — to all three migrated matchers, completing **triple-guard pattern**: negation + modality + evidentiality. **Principle:** if source sentence reports hearsay («Абай ақын болыпты»), promoting it to graph as `(абай, IsA, ақын)` would lose evidential context and recompose hearsay as confirmed knowledge. Adam shouldn't fabricate certainty from reportative source. Refuse extraction. **Implementation:** triple-guard pattern in `copula_is_a`, `nominal_conjunction`, `locative_lives_in` — three sequential guards (negation + modality + Hearsay). All conservative — skip whole matcher on ANY signal. Zero cross-coupling. **Substrate-then-consume cycle: 3 of 4 SemFrame fields with FULLY closed cycles** — Polarity (v4.33.5+v4.34.5), Modality (v4.34.7+v4.35.0), Evidence (v4.36.0+**v4.36.7**); RelationKind remains placeholder. **Corpus impact:** RelatedTo 62 → **56** (-6 from nominal_conjunction Hearsay guard rejecting source sentences with PastEvidential/PastReportative tense — speakers reporting hearsay about relation between two nouns); IsA 1472 unchanged; LivesIn 8 unchanged. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent** unchanged; mean **191.5 ms / 176.1 MB** (-25 ms vs v4.36.6 — likely OS file-cache warmth, triple-guard adds minor hot-path cost); facts.json 1934 → 1928; all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **v4.36.x arc fully complete** — five releases (v4.36.0/.5/.6/.7) closed: third matcher migration + first dialog Hearsay consumption + PastReportative tense + ConverbPerfect/vowel-alternation/short-1sg FST coverage + Evidence extraction guard. The Evidence story is architecturally complete: detection (v4.31.0/v4.36.5), dialog consumption (v4.36.0), extraction refusal (v4.36.7). Pipeline: 3 new guard blocks (~10 lines each) in three matchers + facts regen. Cadence: patch — small uniform change across three matchers. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.37.0 (fourth matcher migration; remaining 6 parser tenses; «X емес пе?» question form); v4.38+ (RelationKind population + consumption).

**v4.36.6 — FST coverage: «алам» short-form 1sg + «оқи» back-vowel converb (final v4.36.x FST gaps closed).** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the two FST coverage gaps re-scoped from v4.36.5 to v4.36.6+. **(1)** «оқи» back-vowel converb — vowel-final back-vowel verbs change shape during converb derivation (оқы → оқи), breaking prefix-match in `surface_could_contain_root`. Pre-fix, surfaces beginning with «оқи*» / «жасы*» / «таны*» couldn't be analysed. **(2)** «алам» short-form 1sg — colloquial Kazakh 1sg present-style verbs drop the `-ын/-ін` tail of personal ending (-мын/-мін → -м). Synth produced only long form, so user-typed «алам / барам / оқим» didn't parse. **Implementation:** **(1)** `surface_could_contain_root` extended with ы/і → и vowel alternation (mirrors existing intervocalic-voicing branch). Synth side already produces «оқи» via `apply_aorist_after_vowel`; gap was purely parser-prefix-match. **(2)** Short-form 1sg synth path inside `try_verb_analyses` nested loop — when feature combo is (Present|PastEvidential) + First + (Sg|None) + polite=false, also try short-form variant by stripping trailing `-ын/-ін` from long-form synth. Limited to 1sg (other persons don't contract in standard Kazakh). **Live verification:** «Оқи» / «Оқиды» now parse (was: no parse); «Алам» / «Барам» now parse with `tense=Present person=First`; «Жаза алам» → "Жақсы екен, сіздің мүмкіндігіңізді түсіндім." (full ability detection works on short form); long forms «аламын» unchanged. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; mean **216.1 ms / 177.1 MB** (+21 ms vs v4.36.5 — real perf cost from vowel-alternation check + short-form synth+compare per matching feature combo; honest trade for closing two architectural gaps); facts 1934 unchanged; all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **v4.36.x arc complete** — three releases (v4.36.0 → v4.36.5 → v4.36.6) closed all v4.36+ FST coverage and consumption work. Hearsay-detection chain now end-to-end functional on natural Kazakh forms across all relevant tense/person variants. Pipeline: 1 extension to `surface_could_contain_root` (~10 lines) + 1 new conditional in `try_verb_analyses` short-form path (~20 lines) + facts version sync. Cadence: patch — two FST gaps closed; honest +21 ms perf cost. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.36.7 (Evidence on extraction side); v4.37.0 (fourth matcher migration; remaining 6 parser tenses; «X емес пе?» question form).

**v4.36.5 — FST coverage: ConverbPerfect + PastReportative («жазыпты» / «болыпты» now route to Hearsay).** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the v4.36.0 honest-gap carry-forward — the «-{Y}п(ты)» reportative form, which is the natural Kazakh hearsay form most commonly produced in user dialog, previously didn't parse at all. **Before:** «Жазыпты» → "Түсінбедім." **After:** "Сізге айтылған сияқты екен — нақты дерегім жоқ." **(1)** New `Tense::PastReportative` variant, distinct from `PastEvidential` (both encode hearsay but differ structurally: PastEvidential = `-ған/-ген` participle base + person endings; PastReportative = `-{Y}п` perfect-converb base + invariant `-ты` particle, no person ending). **(2)** New synth template `VERB_REPORTATIVE_PAST` + match arm in `synthesise_verb`. **(3)** SemFrame maps `PastReportative → Hearsay` alongside existing `PastEvidential → Hearsay`. **(4)** Parser tenses += `ConverbPerfect, PastReportative` (alongside v4.32.5's ConverbImperfect) — closes ConverbPerfect bare form parsing as bonus («жазып» / «беріп» / «оқып» now parse). **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 %** coherent unchanged; mean **194.6 ms / 177.1 MB** (-127 ms vs v4.36.0 — most likely OS file-cache warmth, not true perf improvement; adding 2 tenses costs ~30 % more parse work per verb); facts.json 1935 → 1934 (-1 RelatedTo from new ConverbPerfect parse triggering guard); live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ✓; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ✓; rust_holdout 41/41 ✓; foundation passes. **Live verification:** «Жазыпты» / «Болыпты» / «Абай жазыпты» — all hearsay-aware; «Жазып» (bare ConverbPerfect) now parses; controls («Жазғанмын» PastEvidential / «Жазды» PastDefinite / «Абай жазды») unchanged. **Honest re-scope:** v4.36.5 was originally promised to also close «алам» (short-form 1sg) + «оқи» (back-vowel converb). Those turn out to need separate FST architecture work — «алам» needs short-form personal-ending alternates (invasive); «оқи» needs stem-alternation paradigm matcher (vowel-final back-vowel verbs break prefix-match). Both deferred to v4.36.6+. Pipeline: 1 new Tense variant + 1 synth template + 1 match arm + 1 SemFrame evidence mapping line + 2 parser enumeration entries + facts regen. Cadence: patch — closes one specific architectural gap. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.36.6 («алам» / «оқи» FST fixes); v4.36.7 (Evidence on extraction side); v4.37.0 (fourth matcher migration; remaining 6 parser tenses).

**v4.36.0 — Third matcher migration + first EvidenceKind consumption (Hearsay hedging).** First minor in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Closing the «-ыпты» path is v4.36.5+ FST coverage work. **v4.35.5 — Modal-without-noun: battery case 21 «Жаза аламын» closes.** Patch in v4.35+ semantic-IR arc. Closes battery case 21 — declarative ability claim «Жаза аламын» ("I can write") that has been falling to "Түсінбедім" since v4.32.5 because no `noun_hint` was extracted (verb-only sentence) and v4.34.7's modality routing required both modality AND noun_hint. v4.35.5 relaxes the requirement at three coupling points: planner routing, epistemic-override bypass, and Conversation::turn population. **Before:** «Жаза аламын» → "Түсінбедім." **After:** "Жақсы екен, сіздің мүмкіндігіңізді түсіндім." **(1)** Conversation::turn modality population moved out of noun_hint-Some guard — polarity is per-noun, modality is on lexical verb (independent of noun_hint). **(2)** Planner modality routing relaxed — modality alone routes to appropriate modal family. **(3)** Epistemic-override bypass relaxed — `input_modality: Some(_)` enough to skip override. **(4)** +9 no-noun template variants across 3 modal families. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; **mod-consumed 3/4** (up from 2/4 — case 21 now visible) — case 22 still routes through AskAboutSystem (not modality, gets existing smart honest refusal); neg-consumed 5/5; mean **320.3 ms / 175.9 MB** unchanged; all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Known FST gaps (carry-forward):** «Сөйлей алам» (short 1sg «алам» without -ын not enumerated) + «Оқи аламын» (back-vowel converb «оқи» synthesis) — these are FST coverage gaps in v4.32.5 ConverbImperfect enumeration, deferred to v4.36+ alongside remaining 8 parser tenses. Pipeline: 1 indent change in Conversation::turn + 1 simpler planner conditional + 1 simpler override match arm + 9 template variants. Cadence: patch — closes long-stuck battery case via 3-point relaxation. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.36.0 (third extract_facts matcher migration; first EvidenceKind consumption — Hearsay hedging); v4.36.5 (FST coverage for short «алам» + back-vowel converb); v4.37+ (remaining 8 parser tenses).

**v4.35.0 — Second extract_facts matcher migration + modality guard on extraction side.** First minor in v4.35+ semantic-IR arc. Closes substrate-then-consume cycle for **Modality on the extraction side** (mirroring v4.34.7's dialog-side consumption). Migrates `nominal_conjunction` to consume `&[SemFrame]` (second matcher after `copula_is_a` in v4.34.5). Retroactively adds modality guard to `copula_is_a` for symmetry. Both matchers now refuse extraction when sentence carries either sentence-level negation OR periphrastic modality. **Principle:** modal claims are normative or epistemic, not factual assertions; extracting them as graph facts loses the modal nature. **(1)** `nominal_conjunction` signature: + `sem_frames: &[SemFrame]`. **(2)** Dual guards on `nominal_conjunction`: negation refuses when any noun-class frame has `polarity == Negated`; modality refuses when any frame has `modality.is_some()`. Both conservative — skip whole matcher on ANY signal. **(3)** Retroactive modality guard on `copula_is_a` for symmetry — pre-v4.35.0 had only negation. **(4)** Modality consumption on extraction side closes second substrate-then-consume cycle: Polarity (v4.33.5 dialog + v4.34.5 extraction); Modality (v4.34.7 dialog + **v4.35.0** extraction). **Verification:** Workspace **862 → 865 passing** (+3 unit tests); facts.json **1937 → 1935** (-2 RelatedTo from nominal_conjunction guards rejecting sentences with negation in adjective modifiers; IsA 1472 unchanged); real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 %** coherent unchanged; neg-consumed 5/5; mod-consumed 2/4 (cases 19, 20 visibly modal-aware); mean **320.3 ms / 176.8 MB** (-1.2 ms vs v4.34.7, within noise); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** the 2 rejected RelatedTo facts came from sentences with «емес» as part of an adjective modifier earlier in the sentence (not directly negating the related-to pair) — conservative refusal is the safe move. Pipeline: 1 modality guard for copula_is_a + 1 signature change for nominal_conjunction + 2 guards (negation + modality) + 1 dispatch update + 3 test-site updates + 3 new unit tests + facts regen. Cadence: minor — closes second substrate-then-consume cycle. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.35.5 (modal-without-noun, case 21 «Жаза аламын»; EvidenceKind consumption); v4.36.0 (third matcher migration — likely `locative_lives_in`); v4.37+ (remaining 8 parser tenses; «X емес пе?» question form).

**v4.34.7 — First Modality consumption: per-modality template families (Necessity / Possibility / Ability).** Patch in v4.34+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the substrate-then-consume cycle for the **second** SemFrame field — `Modality`. Populated since v4.32.0 (Necessity / Possibility) + v4.32.5 (Ability), but response generator ignored it. v4.34.7 wires three per-modality template families that engage with the user's modal claim instead of asserting a generic fact about noun_hint. **Before:** «Кітап оқу керек» → "Кітап — әдебиет көзі" (definition ignoring necessity). **After:** «Кітап оқу керек» → "**Иә, маңызды мәселе екен.**" (necessity-aware). **(1)** `Intent::Unknown.input_modality: Option<Modality>` field — second SemFrame-derived field (after v4.33.5's `noun_hint_polarity`). Default None preserves all pre-v4.34.7 routing. **(2)** Conversation::turn populates from any frame in stream (modality is on lexical verb, not noun_hint frame): `*input_modality = sem_frames.iter().find_map(|f| f.modality)`. **(3)** Per-modality planner routing: `Necessity → unknown.with_modal_necessity` / `Possibility → unknown.with_modal_possibility` / `Ability → unknown.with_modal_ability`. Runs AFTER polarity check (negation has higher priority on rare «X V керек емес»). **(4)** Epistemic-override bypass for modality (mirrors v4.34.0's polarity bypass) — when modality set, base_key wins over Tentative/Conflicted overrides. **(5)** 3 new template families with 5 templates each. Necessity: «Иә, маңызды мәселе екен», «Бұл шынымен керек». Possibility: «Мүмкін екен, иә», «Мұндай мүмкіндік бар деп ойлауыңыз орынды». Ability: «Жақсы екен, сіздің мүмкіндігіңізді түсіндім». **Verification:** Workspace **862 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; **mod-consumed 2/4** (cases 19, 20 visibly modal-aware; 21 unchanged — no noun_hint, modal-without-noun is v4.35+ work; 22 unchanged — routes through AskAboutSystem before Unknown branch); neg-consumed 5/5 unchanged; mean **321.5 ms / 176.0 MB** (-2.7 ms vs v4.34.5, within noise); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Substrate-then-consume status:** 2 of 3 SemFrame fields with closed cycles — Polarity (v4.33.5 dialog + v4.34.5 extraction), Modality (v4.34.7 dialog). Evidence + RelationKind still placeholder. Pipeline: 1 new Intent field + 1 semantics propagation + 1 verifier propagation + 5 test-site patches + 1 Conversation::turn population + 1 planner per-modality match + 1 epistemic bypass arm + 3 new template families (15 templates). Cadence: patch — closes second substrate-then-consume cycle. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.35.0 (second extract_facts matcher migration; modality consumption on extraction side); v4.35.5 (modal claims without noun_hint; EvidenceKind consumption); v4.36+ (remaining 8 parser tenses; «X емес пе?» question form).

**v4.34.5 — First extract_facts pattern matcher migration: copula_is_a consumes &[SemFrame], refuses negated extraction.** Patch in v4.34+ semantic-IR arc. Closes a long-standing carry-forward (originally promised v4.32.5, then v4.34.0). First time a corpus-extraction pattern matcher reads from the `&[SemFrame]` stream — substrate-then-consume cycle now closed for the **extraction side** of the pipeline (was already closed for **dialog side** at v4.33.5). As more matchers migrate, they share this single computed stream instead of re-analysing. **(2)** `copula_is_a` signature: + `sem_frames: &[SemFrame]` parameter (old `_parses: &[Analysis]` preserved for sibling-matcher compatibility). **(3)** Negation guard: refuse IsA extraction when any noun-class frame in stream has `polarity == Negated`. Synthetic test: «биология — ғылым емес» pre-v4.34.5 would extract «биология IsA ғылым» (wrong); v4.34.5 refuses ✓. **Substrate-then-consume cycle closed for both sides:** dialog populates v4.33.0 / consumes v4.33.5; extraction populates v4.33.0 (same detector run inside build_sem_frames) / consumes v4.34.5. Modality cycle next (v4.34.7 dialog consumption). **Verification:** Workspace **860 → 862 passing** (+2 copula negation tests); facts.json **1934 → 1937** (+3 from other matchers benefiting from v4.32.5 ConverbImperfect; **IsA count 1472 unchanged** — guard didn't reject any current fact, as audit predicted); real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent** unchanged; neg-consumed 5/5 unchanged; live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ✓; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ✓; rust_holdout 41/41 ✓; foundation passes; mean **324.2 ms / 176.9 MB** RSS (+0.8 ms vs v4.34.0, build_sem_frames overhead, within noise). **What's NOT in v4.34.5:** other matchers (`locative_lives_in`, `dative_goes_to`, `possessive_has`, `nominal_conjunction`, etc.) still take vestigial `_parses` and don't consume sem_frames yet — per-matcher migration in subsequent releases.
