**v4.34.0 — Parser particle-copula extension + epistemic-override polarity bypass (battery edge case 18 closed).** First minor in v4.34+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the FST coverage gap that blocked inflected «емес» forms from parsing AND the planner-routing gap that let `EpistemicStatus::Tentative` override v4.33.5's polarity-aware routing. Together: battery edge case 18 («Сен бағдарламашы емессің бе?»), tracked since the original 2026-05-02 live REPL session that drove v4.30.0, finally gets the response it deserves. **Before:** "Бәлкім, бағдарламашы туралы айтасыз ба." (tentative fallback). **After:** "Бағдарламашы емес деп айтасыз — пікіріңізді сыйлаймын." (respectful acknowledgment). **(1)** Parser surgical branch: `"particle" if entry.root == "емес"` dispatches through `try_noun_analyses` which enumerates Predicate copulas (P1Sg / P2SgInformal / P2SgPolite / P1Pl / P2PlInformal / P2PlPolite). Other particles (ба/бе/ма/ме question particles, да/де connectors) keep bare-only behavior — surgical, minimum blast radius. Bare-form path explicitly preserved. **(2)** Epistemic-override bypass: new first match arm in planner override block — when `noun_hint_polarity == Negated`, return None (preserve base_key from `plan_response_with_session`). Reason: user is denying X's predicate role, not asking for evidence; "tentative" template would force user back into asserting X. Post-fix `[1] бағдарламашы polarity=Negated [2] емес/Function pred=P1Sg` and `[2] pred=P2SgInformal` for «емессің», `pred=P1Pl` for «емеспіз». **Verification:** Workspace **860 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent** (extends v4.33.5's 24 with 2 inflected-negation cases); **Neg-consumed 5/5 = 100 %** (up from 2/5 — cases 18, 25, 26 now route through `unknown.with_negated_topic`); modal-detect 4/4; mean **323.4 ms / 175.9 MB** (+0.9 ms vs v4.33.5, parser cost; within noise); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** closes a 5-version-old carry-forward (battery edge case 18 surfaced 2026-05-02 live REPL, tracked since v4.30.0). Matched architectural pair (parser coverage + planner override priority); either alone wouldn't close the gap. Other particles keep bare-only dispatch — extending them would surface unrelated regressions; per-particle surgical pattern can be added if real REPL surfaces need. Pattern matcher migration deferred to v4.34.5 (closing edge case 18 was higher-visibility; matcher migration would dilute review). Pipeline: 1 parser branch + 1 planner override arm + battery 24→26 + facts version sync. **v4.33.5 — First SemFrame consumption: Polarity::Negated routes Unknown to respectful negation acknowledgment.** Patch in v4.33+ semantic-IR arc, **landmark release** — first time a populated SemFrame field influences user-facing answer text. v4.31.0 → v4.33.0 all populated SemFrame fields without consumption (substrate-then-consume discipline). v4.33.5 starts consumption: when user negates a topic with «X емес», response generator no longer asserts a definition contradicting the user's claim. **Before:** «Бұл шындық емес» → "Шындық — ең күшті қару" (definition that contradicts user). **After:** «Бұл шындық емес» → "Шындық емес деп айтасыз — пікіріңізді сыйлаймын" (respectful acknowledgment). **(1)** `Intent::Unknown.noun_hint_polarity: Polarity` field — first SemFrame-derived field on canonical Intent type; default Affirmative preserves all pre-v4.33.5 routing exactly. **(2)** `Conversation::turn` walks sem_frames for the frame whose root matches noun_hint, copies polarity. SemFrame build moved earlier in turn pipeline (was at trace-assembly time; now right after parses). **(3)** Planner short-circuit: when `noun_hint_polarity == Negated && noun_hint.is_some()`, route to `unknown.with_negated_topic` BEFORE all other Unknown-routing — overrides "I have evidence about X" paths because user is denying X's predicate role. **(4)** New template family `unknown.with_negated_topic` in v1.toml — 5 templates echoing user's negation back («{noun} емес деп айтасыз...») framed as respectful acknowledgment with «пікіріңіз / ойыңыз» marking epistemic status as user-asserted. **Verification:** Workspace **860 passing** unchanged (14 Intent::Unknown test-site patches mechanically added default-Affirmative); real-world **24-query battery 24/24 = 100 % coherent** (up from 23/24 — cases 23, 24 now contextually correct); **neg-consumed 2/2 = 100 %** — first SemFrame field consumption metric; mean **322.5 ms / 175.1 MB** RSS (matched v4.33.0; -1.9 MB, slight noise improvement); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Substrate-then-consume cycle closed for polarity:** v4.31.0 type → v4.31.5 trace visibility → v4.33.0 population → v4.33.5 consumption. **v4.33.0 — Sentence-level negation: «X емес» → Polarity::Negated on prior noun.** First minor in v4.33+ semantic-feature population arc. Closes the noun-polarity gap left by v4.31.0 — `Polarity` was unified across nouns and verbs but only auto-derived from `VerbFeatures.negation` (verb-level). v4.33.0 adds sentence-level detection: when a noun-class frame is followed by «емес» («not») particle, the noun's polarity flips to `Negated`. The Kazakh polarity story is now architecturally complete for non-inflected patterns. **(1)** `populate_sentential_negation(&mut [SemFrame])` — single linear scan; for each `frame[i].root == "емес"`, mark `frame[i-1].polarity = Negated` if predecessor is noun-like (Noun / Adjective / Pronoun / Numeral). Verb frames skipped (their negation comes from `VerbFeatures.negation`, FST-level). **(2)** Wired into `turn_with_trace` AFTER ability detection. Live: «Бұл шындық емес» → `[1] шындық/Noun polarity=Negated`; «Ол ұзын емес» → `[1] ұзын/Adjective polarity=Negated`. Negation attaches to immediate predecessor (the actual content head), not to leading pronoun. **(3) Known FST gap (carry-forward to v4.34+):** inflected forms «емеспін / емессің / емеспіз / емессіз» do NOT parse — `parser::analyse` dispatches `particle` POS through catch-all branch (bare-only). «Мен X емеспін» loses the inflected token; detection blocked until parser's particle dispatch is extended to enumerate predicate copulas. Documented as v4.34+ prerequisite. **Verification:** Workspace **854 → 860 passing** (+6 negation tests: bare-noun, leading-pronoun-attachment, verb-skip, no-match negative, position-zero skipped, idempotence); real-world **24-query battery 23/24 = 95.8 %** coherent (no regression vs v4.32.5; case 21 still honest "Түсінбедім" on declarative ability); **modal-detect 4/4**, **neg-detect 2/2**; mean **322.5 ms / 177.0 MB** RSS (-2.9 ms vs v4.32.5, within noise — negation detection adds zero measurable cost); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** Polarity::Negated populated on noun frames in canonical pattern but **not yet consumed** by response generator — text unchanged. Polarity-aware response generation is v4.33.5+ work. The polarity story is now architecturally complete: verbs derive from FST-level `VerbFeatures.negation`; nouns/adjectives derive from sentential «емес» (this release). Pipeline: 1 new function (~40 lines) + 1 re-export + 1 turn_with_trace line + 6 unit tests + battery 22→24 + facts version sync. Cadence: minor — closes meaningful gap that v4.31.0 deliberately left for a future release. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.33.5 (first consumption of SemFrame fields — template branching on Polarity + Modality); v4.34.0 (parser particle-copula extension + first extract_facts pattern matcher migration to `&[SemFrame]`); v4.35+ (remaining 8 parser tenses; battery edge case 18 «X емес пе?» question form).

**v4.32.5 — Ability `-а ал-` detection + parser tense expansion (ConverbImperfect).** Patch in v4.32+ semantic-feature population arc — closes the third member of the Kazakh modality triad. Fixing both together is the matched architectural pair. **(1)** `parser::try_verb_analyses` tense enumeration += `ConverbImperfect`. Other 8 missing tenses (ConverbPerfect, 3 participles, FutureIntentional, FuturePossible, Conditional, Imperative) deferred to releases that need them. **(2)** `populate_ability_modality(&mut [SemFrame])` with **dual-signal check**: signal (a) current frame's `root == "ал"` AND `pos == Verb`; signal (b) preceding frame's `tense == Some(ConverbImperfect)`. Both required — eliminates false positive on «Кітапты алдым» ("I took the book") where `ал` is just the regular transitive verb. **(3)** Wired into `turn_with_trace` AFTER `populate_periphrastic_modality`; first-detection-wins. **v4.32.0 — Modality population from periphrastic auxiliaries (керек / тиіс / мүмкін).** First minor in v4.32+ semantic-feature population arc, second SemFrame consumer migration. **v4.31.5 — SemFrame consumer #1: TurnTrace.sem_frames + --trace renderer; +real-world battery + RSS measurement.** Patch in v4.31+ semantic-IR arc. First consumer migration of v4.31.0's SemFrame substrate, plus the start of a new release-discipline practice: every release tested with **real human-like Kazakh queries**, reporting both latency AND max RSS per query (not just templated holdout pass-rates). **(1)** `TurnTrace.sem_frames: Vec<SemFrame>` field — populated in `turn_with_trace` via `parses.iter().map(SemFrame::from).collect()`; one frame per parse, lossless conversion. **(2)** `adam_chat --trace` SemFrame renderer — compact one-line-per-frame format showing polarity / evidence / modality auto-derivations live. Example for «Кітапты оқымадым»: `[1] оқы/Verb tense=PastDefinite person=First polarity=Negated` — proves the v4.31.0 negation→Polarity::Negated auto-derivation flows end-to-end through the trace boundary. **(3)** Real-world 18-query battery: **mean 322.7 ms / query · mean 176.8 MB RSS · 18/18 = 100 % coherent responses** across small_talk / identity / capabilities / knowledge / rust / honest_unknown / edge categories. Each measured via `/usr/bin/time -l ./target/release/adam_chat --once "<query>"` (cold-spawn, real-user-shell experience; per-turn hot-loop latency on M2 still 1.07 ms by criterion bench). **Memory baseline correction:** `docs/performance.md` headline RSS updated from stale "~76–80 MB" to current **~177 MB** — the 100 MB growth across v4.29 → v4.31 driven mainly by RootAffinity matrix (26 MB JSON → ~50 MB HashMap), v4.28.5 corpus expansion (~30 MB morpheme index), world_core growth, suffix_priors. Hot-loop per-turn cost unchanged (still 1.07 ms); cold-start dominates `--once`-style invocations. **Verification:** Workspace **839 passing** unchanged; battery **18/18 = 100 %**; live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32; rust_holdout 41/41; foundation passes; memory regression vs v4.31.0 within noise (~0.03 MB from sem_frames Vec). **Carry-forwards:** v4.32.0 (Modality from periphrastic constructions; RelationKind from pattern matchers); v4.32.5 (SemFrame as input to `copula_is_a` matcher — first behavioural migration); v4.33.0+ (sentence-level «X емес» → Negated on prior noun); v4.40+ (battery edge case 18: structural answer to «емес пе?» negation questions). Pipeline: 1 TurnTrace field + 1 turn_with_trace line + ~50-line trace renderer + 18-query battery in CHANGELOG + performance.md RSS update. Cadence: patch — small consumer migration but the release-discipline change (real-world battery + RSS measurement per release) is durable. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer continues.**

**v4.31.0 — Morphemic-logical IR (SemFrame) substrate.** First minor in v4.31+ semantic-IR arc — the architectural step the 2026-05-02 Codex consultation correctly identified as next. Converts agglutination from a tokenizer-improvement into the **internal logic of the system** by introducing a single typed semantic frame that carries each word's full morphological + logical features through the pipeline downstream of FST. v4.31.0 ships **substrate only** — type + lossless conversion + 8 unit tests. No consumers wired (substrate-first pattern, mirror of v4.0.37 → v4.0.38). **(1)** New `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/sem_frame.rs` (~520 lines + 8 tests). Defines `SemFrame { root, pos, case, number, possessive, predicate, derivation, tense, person, voice, polarity, polite, modality, evidence, relation }` plus closed enums `PosTag` / `Polarity` / `Modality` / `EvidenceKind` / `RelationKind`. **(2)** `SemFrame::from_analysis(&Analysis)` + `impl From<&Analysis>` — lossless: every NounFeatures / VerbFeatures field flows through. Auto-derives `polarity = Negated` when `VerbFeatures.negation == true`; `evidence = Some(Hearsay)` when `Tense::PastEvidential`; nouns default `Affirmative` polarity (sentence-level «X емес» is v4.32+). `Modality` and `RelationKind` are placeholder slots for v4.32+ work — always `None` in v4.31.0. **(3)** Re-exports in lib.rs: `SemFrame`, `PosTag`, `Polarity`, `Modality`, `EvidenceKind`, `RelationKind` — single import for downstream crates. **Verification:** Workspace **831 → 839 passing** (+8 SemFrame tests: noun roundtrip, verb roundtrip, negation→Negated, PastEvidential→Hearsay, POS projection covers all 5 classes + Function fallback, polite verb preserved, trait equivalence, determinism); live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ✓; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ✓; rust_holdout 41/41 ✓; foundation passes. **Runtime behaviour change: zero.** v4.31.0 adds the type but wires zero consumers — bit-for-bit identical to v4.30.5. **What this is NOT:** not a runtime change (consumer migration starts v4.31.5); not a deletion of Analysis (SemFrame is a higher-level wrapping); not a neural component. Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 mod registration + 6 re-exports + facts version sync. Cadence: minor — first release of a new architectural primitive that will flow through every downstream consumer over the v4.31.x arc. **Stripe (9) — semantic IR layer opens.** Next: **v4.31.5** (first consumer — extend `--trace` to emit SemFrame per parsed token, OR migrate one extract_facts matcher); **v4.32.0** (populate modality from periphrastic constructions; populate relation from pattern matchers); **v4.33.0+** (sentence-level «X емес» detection; SemFrame as canonical SearchGraph query input).

**v4.30.5 — Precision sweep: DoesTo extraction disabled; +engineering thesis in README; +unified KPI.** Patch in v4.30+ dialog-coherence arc, prompted by 2026-05-02 strategic consultation. **(1)** `patterns::agent_verb` (DoesTo extractor) DISABLED in production pipeline. Audit found 125 / 196 = **64 % of corpus-extracted relations** came from this single matcher (`X Y-ні V-лайды`); review confirmed pairs were surface verbal-phrase co-occurrences, not stable relations: «жаңбыр does_to жер», «ксро does_to байланыс», «рет does_to ел». Function and its 4 unit tests preserved for future semantic-class-filtered re-enable. **Result:** 196 → 71 Grammar facts (-64 %); HumanApproved share rises **90.5 % → 96.3 %** of committed graph. **(2)** Engineering thesis subsection added to README — makes the project's claim explicit and provable: agglutinative morphology gives a clean algebra of meaning (root + typed suffix operators), composition is rule-bound, that's what we build on. Same engineering style applies to Turkish/Kyrgyz/Tatar/Uzbek without claims of universal grammar or historical primacy. **(3)** Unified KPI in `docs/performance.md`: `latency_ms_per_correct_answer = p50_turn_latency_ms / holdout_pass_rate` folds speed + correctness into one comparable number; pass-rate denominator is full workspace test count, so adding 50 tests but dropping one has a measurably worse cost-per-correct even at unchanged latency. v4.30.5 baseline: **1.07 ms / correct answer**. **Verification:** Workspace **831 passing** unchanged; facts.json 2059 → 1934 (exact -125 DoesTo drop); HumanApproved 90.5 % → 96.3 %; live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ✓; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ✓; rust_holdout 41/41 ✓; foundation validation passes. **What this is NOT:** not a fix for the bigger precision risk at 10k+-fact auto-extraction scale (v4.31+ topic if we ramp); not a deletion of `agent_verb` (kept for future semantic-class-filtered re-enable); not the morphemic-logical IR work — that's v4.31.0. Pipeline: 1 line commented + extensive rationale + 1 README subsection + 1 performance.md section + facts regen. Cadence: patch — gigienic correction without architectural change. **Stripe (8) — multi-turn coherence layer continues.** Next: **v4.31.0 — morphemic-logical IR (SemFrame)**, the architectural step Codex correctly identified.

**v4.30.0 — Coreference layer + Rust extraction patches: live REPL 2026-05-02 regressions closed.** First minor in v4.30+ dialog-coherence arc. A 2026-05-02 live REPL session surfaced three failures: (1) «Rust бағдарламалау тілі туралы не білесіз?» extracted topic «тіл» instead of «Rust»; (2) «Раст» (Cyrillic) had no alias; (3) follow-up «Бұл тілдегі кілт сөздер?» couldn't resolve `бұл тіл` to the prior Rust topic — v4.13.0 handled bare-pronoun anaphors but not adnominal demonstratives. v4.30.0 closes all three. **(1)** New `latin_with_generic_head_marker` matches «{LATIN_TECH_SUBJECT} (бағдарламалау|программалау)? {generic head} {topic marker}» and returns the Latin head directly — short-circuits the multiword scanner («бағдарламалау тілі») and topic_marker_hint («тіл») which both extracted the wrong constituent. 9 generic heads × 4 markers × 0–1 qualifier. **(2)** New `input_contains_adnominal_demonstrative` recognises «{бұл/осы/сол} + {generic head}» as a coreference signal; `input_contains_discourse_anaphor` now fires for both bare pronouns (v4.13.0) AND adnominal demonstratives (v4.30.0). The downstream `dialog_context.resolve_anaphor()` path resolves both signals identically. **(3)** programming_rust.jsonl += rust_180 (`Раст` Cyrillic alias) + rust_181 (programming-language list-summary). **(4)** MULTIWORD_ENTITIES += «rust тізімі». **(5)** New `data/eval/live_holdout_2026_05_02.json` (5 cases) + dedicated test rig with **multi-turn `context_turns` support** — first multi-turn case in the holdout suite (demonstrative-coreference case requires prior Rust establishment). **Verification:** Workspace tests **830 → 831 passing** (+1 holdout); live_holdout_2026_05_02 **5/5 = 100 %**; live_holdout_2026_05_01 **32/32 ✓**; rust_holdout **41/41 ✓**; foundation validation passes. **What's NOT solved (carry-forwards):** plural-form multiword («Қандай бағдарламалау тілдерін білесіз?» still falls through — needs morpho-aware multiword scanning or list-intent trigger on «қандай ... білесіз») → v4.30.5+; functional/compositional queries («Бұл тілде функцияны қалай жазамыз?») — coreference resolves but no curated Rust+function entry → v4.31+ compositional-reasoning track; physics domain (zero curated entries) → v4.30.5+. **Honest framing:** this release closes the three failures the user surfaced and adds the first-ever multi-turn coreference path (bare pronouns + adnominal demonstratives now both flow through `dialog_context.resolve_anaphor()`). Subjective "context retention" should improve on follow-up questions; subjective "intelligence" doesn't improve because the system still does retrieval+ranking, not synthesis — that gap is on v4.31+. Pipeline: 1 recogniser + 1 coreference detector + 1 MULTIWORD + 2 world_core + 1 holdout JSON + 1 test rig + facts regen. Cadence: minor — first dialog-coherence-arc release. **Stripe (8) — multi-turn coherence layer.** Next: v4.30.5 (plural-multiword + physics_school seed), v4.31.0 (compositional reasoning).

**v4.29.5 — Track A Phase 2: RootAffinity wired into runtime SearchGraph reranking.** Phase 2 of v4.29.0's Track A — runtime integration of the PMI matrix shipped as a deferred-wiring artifact. **(1)** New `Conversation::with_root_affinity(affinity)` builder mirroring v4.15.5's `with_suffix_priors`; optional, when not attached ranking is bit-for-bit identical to v4.29.0. **(2)** `ToolContext.root_affinity: Option<&RootAffinity>` field threaded through every `Conversation::turn` so each `SearchGraph` dispatch sees the matrix. **(3)** Affinity tier inserted at the **deepest semantic depth** — after `length`, before lexicographic. Initial draft placed it between `domain_match` and `length`, but the `world_core_water` holdout regression revealed that PMI cultural co-occurrence (`су ↔ сусын` in food-context corpus) can outrank length, which is a strong "informativeness" signal. The deepest placement preserves all v4.29.0 ranking outcomes while still firing on truly equivalent candidates — exactly the use case PMI was trained for. **(4)** Live `adam_chat` startup wiring loads `data/retrieval/root_affinity.json` if present; logs `"adam-chat: root affinity — {n_roots} roots, {n_pairs} pairs over {n_samples} training samples"`. Missing file or schema mismatch is non-fatal. **(5)** Holdout test rigs (`live_holdout`, `rust_holdout`) load the matrix when present so the regression suite runs in production-shape configuration. **Ranking ladder post-v4.29.5:** `list_intent_rank → overlap → predicate_priority → domain_match → length DESC → root_affinity DESC ← NEW → lexicographic ASC`. **Verification:** Workspace tests **829 → 830 passing** (+1 new `search_graph_root_affinity_breaks_length_tie` proves the tier flips an alphabetically-losing candidate when PMI is decisive); live_holdout 32/32 ✓ with affinity ON; rust_holdout 41/41 ✓ with affinity ON; **9-query live ON-vs-OFF probe all bit-identical** (the tier is conservative on current world_core where length usually disambiguates — production benefits accumulate as curated graph grows length-tied candidates). **Honest limitation:** the matrix was trained over a corpus dominated by general/news/textbook contexts; specialty-domain PMI (chemistry, medicine, programming) is sparse — bridging this is on the v4.30+ roadmap. Pipeline: 1 builder + 1 ToolContext field + 1 ranking tier + 1 unit test + adam_chat load wiring + 2 holdout test load wirings + facts/derived_facts version sync. Cadence: patch — runtime integration of an already-shipped artifact, conservative tier placement. **Stripe (7) — Track A discourse-prior layer.** Next: v4.30.0 (per-domain PMI matrices + cross-turn topic carry via previous_grounded_fact + Result-ты Accusative-with-dash tokenizer fix).

**v4.29.0 — Track A discourse-level prior: RootAffinity (PMI matrix) — 834k pairs across 10 523 roots.** First minor in v4.29+ Track A discourse-level statistical layer. v4.15 → v4.20 built SuffixPriors for chain-level morphology disambiguation. v4.28.5 expanded corpus 5.77M → 8.85M tokens. v4.29.0 ships **first cross-word semantic signal**: sparse PMI matrix over root pairs that co-occur in same sample. **Phase 1 only — artifact + type + training binary**; runtime integration deferred to v4.29.5. **(1)** New module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/root_affinity.rs` (~250 lines + 5 unit tests). `RootAffinity { version, trained_on_samples, min_pair_count, root_log_prob, pair_pmi }` — sparse map indexed `outer_root → inner_root → PMI` with lex-smaller-first key normalization. **(2)** Why PMI not raw count: raw co-occurrence dominated by ubiquitous roots (мен/ол/бір) — produce no signal. PMI normalizes by marginals: `log(P(a,b) / (P(a)·P(b)))`. Filter `MIN_PAIR_COUNT = 5` suppresses small-sample noise. **(3)** New training binary `train_root_affinity.rs` — three-pass algorithm (collect samples → FST-analyse unique tokens → walk samples accumulating single+pair counts). Output: `data/retrieval/root_affinity.json` byte-stable sorted. **Trained on v4.28.5 corpus:** 1,076,271 samples / 10,523 roots / 3,389,957 pairs pre-filter / **834,053 pairs post-filter** (24.6% survival) / 6,662 outer roots / 26 MB JSON / ~1.5 min training time. **Sample affinities:** жасуша↔ядро=4.29, атом↔ядро=4.28, бала↔ана=2.11, тау↔көл=2.09, кітап↔ілім=1.03, жер↔күн=0.50, rust↔cargo=0.0 (Latin not in Kazakh lexicon → handled separately). **Verification:** Workspace tests **824 → 829 passing** (+5 root_affinity unit tests); rust_holdout 41/41 ✓; live_holdout 32/32 ✓; parse-disambig 23/23 ✓; 80-q battery 79/80 (zero behavior change since Phase 1). **What v4.29.5 will enable:** `Conversation::with_root_affinity(...)` builder mirroring `with_suffix_priors`; `current_topic_root` in ToolContext; affinity tiebreaker in `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` ranking ladder. Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 new binary + 1 new artifact + facts version sync. Cadence: minor — first artifact in new prior axis (chain → root pair). Architectural addition, zero runtime behavior change. **Stripe (7) — Track A corpus expansion → discourse-prior layer.** Next: v4.29.5 (runtime integration of RootAffinity into reranking).

**v4.25.0 — R5 degree-based hub filter (Codex actionable #5): −75.5 % derived facts, holdout still 100 %.** First minor in v4.25+ engineering-hygiene arc. Closes 5th Codex review actionable. Pre-fix, **22931/25006 = 91.7 %** of derived facts came from a single rule (`R5_shared_is_a_target`: A IsA X ∧ B IsA X ⟹ RelatedTo(A, B)) — Codex identified this as source of tangential-answer risk. The v4.0.23 named-list filter only caught 5 categorical-abstract hubs (зат/белгі/әрекет/құбылыс/адам); the long tail of mid-degree hubs (10–50 incoming IsA each) generated cartesian-product RelatedTo pairs (𝑑·(𝑑−1)/2) that crowded the derivation pool without dialog-relevant value. **(1)** New `MAX_R5_HUB_DEGREE = 8` constant in `crates/adam-reasoning/src/reasoner.rs`. Any hub with > 8 incoming IsA edges is skipped wholesale. Structural complement to the named filter — runs before the cartesian-product loop. **(2)** Threshold tuned empirically against the v4.24.5 live holdout: chosen so all `unknown.with_derived_chain` fixtures continue to produce a derivation (no «байланыс-» template variant goes red) and live_holdout stays at 100 %, while reduction is large enough to materially change pool composition. **Impact:** Total derived facts **25 006 → 6 137 (−18 869, −75.5 %)**; R5 derivations **22 931 → 1 159 (−95.0 %)**; R5 share **91.7 % → 18.9 %**; `derived_facts.json` ~14 MB → ~3.5 MB. **Verification:** Workspace tests **823 → 823 passing**; live holdout **32/32 = 100.0 %**; parse-disambig eval still **23/23 = 100 %**. The reduction is entirely tangential bloat that no existing test actually consumed. **Why this matters beyond the metric:** with 22 931 R5 derivations dominating the candidate pool, retrieval ranking had a structural bias toward surfacing RelatedTo chains over curated direct facts. v4.25.0 shrinks the pool the ranker sees from ~25 K → ~6 K candidates. Sets up domain-aware scoring (the second half of Codex's recommendation) to be a smaller follow-up patch. Pipeline: 1 constant + 1 skip branch (~30-line addition) + artifact regeneration. No schema diff, no API change, no template change. **v4.24.5 — live holdout eval (Codex actionable #4): blind substring-based regression baseline.** Patch in v4.24+ engineering-hygiene arc. **v4.22.0 — runtime integration of chain_tiebreak_root: priors+root infrastructure now reaches live dialog.** First minor in v4.22+ runtime-integration arc. v4.19.0 → v4.21.5 built the parse-disambiguation eval framework, surfaced the chain-collision blind spot, added root-level priors with closed-class boost, and shipped the FST pronoun-paradigm matcher — closing the eval at 100 % across 23 cases. **But that 100 % only applied inside the eval binary.** The actual dialog runtime (`parse_input_inner` in `adam-dialog`) was still using chain-only smoothed scoring without the root tiebreak. v4.22.0 closes the loop. **(1)** Runtime comparator in `parse_input_inner` extended — chain-prior re-rank gains a root-tiebreaker tier (`chain_diff < EPSILON` → `score_root(root)` decides). Same logic as the eval's `pick_chain_with_root_tiebreak` from v4.20.0; `EPSILON = 1e-4` matches eval. **(2)** Strictly additive on the no-priors path — when `priors: None` is passed, the comparator block is skipped entirely; `parse_input` returns the v3.2.0 deterministic order bit-for-bit. **(3)** Three new runtime regression tests in `runtime_priors_tests` — load real frozen artifact + lexicon and assert production parse picks gold pronoun root for онда → ол, маған → мен, саған → сен. Plus a no-priors equivalence test. **What does NOT change:** 8 eval strategies in eval_parse_disambiguation unchanged (`chain_tiebreak_root` still 23/23 = 100 %, chain-only still 21/23 = 91.3 %); all non-pronoun workspace tests preserve v4.16.0 behaviour exactly (chain-difference cases are the 99 % of dialog); public API surface (`parse_input_with_priors` signature) identical. Pipeline: ~30-line comparator extension + 4 unit tests; no schema changes, no new artifacts, no new dependencies. Workspace tests **818 → 822 passing** (+4 runtime priors tests). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — runtime layer opens.** Next: v4.22.5+ (live REPL transcript collection to verify chain-collision improvements show up in real dialog), v4.23.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog).

**v4.21.5 — pronoun paradigm extension (бұл / сол / мен / сен) + 4 new eval cases + сол lexicon entry.** Patch in v4.21+ FST irregularity arc. v4.21.0 shipped ол's 6 oblique cases as the architectural foundation; v4.21.5 extends the same mechanism to the rest of the demonstrative / personal closed class. **(1)** Paradigm table grew 6 → 21 entries: бұл (6 oblique cases — same `л → н/ғ/д` lateralization), сол (6 cases — same pattern), мен (only Dative маған — others regular), сен (only Dative саған — same `сен → са-` alternation). **(2)** `data/tokenizer/segmentation_roots.json` += `pron_sol` — uncovered while running new сол eval cases: `analyse("соған")` previously returned only verb-root «соға» (Reflexive paradigm) parses, no «сол + Dat», because бare сол wasn't in the lexicon at all (despite being a top-tier demonstrative pronoun). 1-line lexicon fix. **(3)** Eval test set extended +4 cases: bunda_anaphoric (бұл Loc), sogan_dative (сол Dat), magan_dative (мен Dat), sagan_dative (сен Dat). **(4)** Frozen priors artifact regenerated — closed-class boost now applies to 6 of 10 entries (was 5 at v4.20.5; сол newly included). **Results (n=23):** baseline 78.3 %; chain-only strategies 91.3 % (improved from 89.5 % at v4.21.0 — chain priors handle most new cases without root help, because pronoun parses have higher chain prior scores than content-word alternatives); **chain_tiebreak_root 23/23 = 100.0 %**. **v4.21.0 — pronoun stem-alternation paradigm + 100 % accuracy on parse-disambiguation eval.** First minor in v4.21+ FST irregularity arc. v4.20.5's debug pass surfaced the actionable diagnosis: the FST returned no parse with root=`ол` for «онда» because Kazakh's phonological alternation `ол → он-` (lateralization `л → н` before consonant-initial dental suffixes) wasn't modelled. v4.21.0 ships the irregularity as a small hardcoded paradigm matcher and **closes the entire v4.19.0–v4.20.5 measurement arc with `chain_tiebreak_root` reaching 100 % accuracy on the parse-disambiguation eval**. **(1)** New module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/pronoun_paradigm.rs` — irregular-form table for Kazakh pronouns. v4.21.0 ships the `ол` paradigm (онда / оны / оның / оған / одан / онымен — 6 oblique cases). **(2)** `try_pronoun_paradigm(surface, lex)` consulted by `analyse()` after the regular noun/verb passes — strictly additive, no disturbance of existing candidates. The bare pronoun root is looked up via `lex.get(...)`; missing lexicon entry degrades silently. **Why hardcoded table not phonology rule:** general allomorph rules `л → н/ғ/д` would over-trigger on consonant-final nouns (ел → *ен-, бел → *бен-); linguistic reality is closed-class irregularity, exactly captured by listing the surface forms. **(3)** `pronoun_paradigm` exported from lib.rs for downstream extension. **(4)** Frozen priors artifact regenerated — онда tokens now produce 2 distinct roots, correctly classified as ambiguous and skipped from root counting; closed-class boost (×10 from v4.20.5) keeps `P(ол)=-3.24 > P(он)=-5.06`. **Results (n=19):** baseline 78.9 %; chain-only strategies 89.5 %; chain_plus_root 94.7 %; **chain_tiebreak_root 100.0 %** — both онда cases (sentence-initial + mid-sentence) now correctly resolve to ол. **+21.1pp absolute lift over baseline.** This release closes a 6-release arc (v4.19.0 → v4.21.0) that surfaced and resolved the chain-collision blind spot. The combined system: chain priors handle regular cases; root priors + closed-class boost provide the chain-collision tiebreaker; FST stem-alternation makes closed-class oblique forms available as candidates. Each layer has clear responsibility, clear-typed artifact, transparent eval reporting. Pipeline: 1 new module + 5 unit tests + analyse() augmented + lib.rs exports + artifact regen + eval JSON RESOLVED notes. Workspace tests **809→814 passing** (+5 pronoun_paradigm). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — measurement layer CLOSED at 100 %.** Next: v4.21.5 (extend paradigm with бұл / сол / мен / сен / мынау / анау + new eval cases), v4.22.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog).

**v4.20.5 — closed-class structural-pronoun boost + diagnostic discovery: онда's gold parse isn't an FST candidate.** Patch in v4.20+ root-axis arc. Implements the closed-class boost planned by v4.20.0's writeup, then surfaces the **third (and most actionable) negative finding**: priors-side fixes were targeting the wrong layer the entire time. **(1) New** `data/lexicon/closed_class_root_boosts.json` — hand-curated multiplicative count boosts for structural pronouns (ол/бұл/сол/мен/сен/олар/біз/сіз/осы/мынау/анау). Compensates for v4.20.0's pronoun under-counting. **(2)** Training binary updated — reads boost file (graceful fallback), applies multiplicative factor to `root_counts` AFTER unambiguous-only counting and BEFORE Laplace smoothing. **No schema bump** (still v4) — boost folds into existing `root_log_prob`. **(3)** Eval binary `ADAM_DEBUG_TIEBREAK=1` env-gated debug pass dumps per-parse chain key, chain score, root score, picked parse. **Boost validation:** `ол` flipped from -5.45 → **-3.24** (now above `он` at -5.06); `бұл`: -5.09 → -3.10; `сен`: -6.96 → -5.44. 5 of 10 boosted roots applied (other 5 never appeared unambiguously). Boost mechanism works as designed. **THE CRITICAL FINDING:** eval results unchanged — `chain_tiebreak_root` STILL picks `он` for both онда cases. The debug logger reveals why: **the FST returns NO parse with `root=ол` for «онда»**. Both candidates have `root=он`. The gold parse isn't even a candidate. Reason: «онда» starts with «он», not «ол». The FST's prefix-match on root surface forms never considers «ол» (2 chars) for «онда» (4 chars). Kazakh has phonological alternation `ол → он-` before consonant-initial suffixes (locative `-да`, accusative `-ны`, dative `-ған`) — regular lateralization. The lexicon has bare `ол` as a pronoun root, but the FST has no machinery to generate the `он-` allomorph during analysis. **Implication:** three releases of priors-side architecture (v4.19.0/v4.19.5/v4.20.0/v4.20.5) were looking in the wrong layer. The priors infrastructure stays in place for genuine chain-collision cases — but the онда case can only be fixed at the FST/lexicon layer, not the scoring layer. This finding *unblocks* the project: eliminates an entire class of priors-tuning that would have continued to fail. Pipeline: 1 new data file + training binary boost-pass + eval debug logger + eval JSON notes updated. Workspace tests **809→809 passing**. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — root axis layer continues, but next step pivots OFF priors.** Next: v4.20.10 / v4.21.0 (FST stem-alternation for pronoun paradigm — add `он-`/`оғ-`/`соған-`/`маған-` allomorphs so онда/оған/маған/бұнда surface the correct pronoun root as a candidate). Once the gold parse is *available*, v4.20.0's root prior + v4.20.5's closed-class boost will pick it under `chain_tiebreak_root` — at which point онда finally flips.

**v4.20.0 — root-level priors + new prior axis (P(root) marginals via unambiguous-only attribution).** First minor in v4.20+ root-axis arc. v4.19.5 surfaced the structural finding that chain-level priors can't disambiguate root identity when both parses share a chain (онда: `он+Loc` and `ол+Loc` collide). v4.20.0 builds the missing axis: a root-level marginal `P(root)` over the corpus, trained via **unambiguous-only attribution**, with two new evaluation strategies that combine it with the chain prior. **The empirical result is itself the second negative finding in a row** — but the architectural foundation is in place, the failure mode is precisely diagnosed, and the next steps are sharp. **(1) Schema bump v3 → v4** — new `SuffixPriors::root_log_prob` field; `load()` rejects v3. **(2) New constructor `from_counts_with_bigrams_and_roots`** — third axis on top of v4.16/4.17 chain+bigram+POS. **(3) New method `score_root(root)`** — log P(root) with Laplace smoothing and floor. Empty-priors path returns 0.0 (additive identity). **(4) Training binary updated** — root counts via **unambiguous-only attribution**: token contributes to root only when `analyse()` returns parses with a single distinct root. Per v4.19.5 finding, uniform 1/N would dilute chain-collision pairs (онда → 0.5 он + 0.5 ол) — exactly where tiebreaker is needed. **(5) Frozen artifact regenerated** at schema v4: 1112 chains, **9338 roots** from 3.3M unambiguous-token instances, 530K ambiguous skipped (~13.9% ambiguity rate). 1.5 MB JSON. **(6) Two new eval strategies:** `chain_plus_root` (additive log-prob), `chain_tiebreak_root` (strict tiebreaker). **Results (n=19):** baseline 78.9%; chain-only strategies 89.5%; **chain_plus_root REGRESSES to 84.2%** (high-frequency root «нелік» overrides correct chain pick); **chain_tiebreak_root holds at 89.5%** (no regression but no lift on онда). **Why онда still doesn't flip:** unambiguous-only attribution systematically under-counts pronouns. `ол` appears mostly in inherently-ambiguous forms (онда, оны, оған) which get filtered; digit `он` appears in many unambiguous numeric contexts (dates, ages). Result: corpus marginal `P(он) > P(ол)`, even though pronoun is far more common in real Kazakh. Fix paths: **closed-class boost** (v4.20.5 — hand-curate ол/бұл/сол/мен/сен/олар/біз/сіз with explicit prior boost), **lexical co-occurrence** `P(root | surrounding tokens)` (v4.21.0+), or **dialog-layer anaphor resolution** (bigger lift). Pipeline: schema v3→v4 + 1 new field + 1 new constructor + 1 new method + 2 unit tests + training binary updated + frozen artifact regenerated + 2 new eval strategies. Workspace tests **807→809 passing**. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — root axis layer opens.** Next: v4.20.5 (closed-class structural-pronoun boost), v4.21.0+ (lexical co-occurrence if needed).

**v4.19.5 — sentence-context strategy + structural finding on root-vs-chain disambiguation.** Patch in v4.19+ measurement arc. v4.19.0 surfaced one residual failure («онда» — gold = `ол + Loc` anaphoric, all isolated-token strategies pick `он + Loc` "in ten") and tagged it as needing "FST sentence-context plumbing." v4.19.5 builds that strategy and measures whether it actually helps. **It does not.** Publishable negative result — the structural reason gives a clearer architectural direction than blindly adding more context layers. **(1)** New `with_context` strategy as 6th tier in `eval_parse_disambiguation`: walks the full eval sentence left-to-right, greedily picking each token's parse under bigram-aware Jelinek-Mercer smoothed scoring (mirrors `parse_input_inner` in `adam-dialog`), tracks `prev_chain` across tokens, returns the root that won when target token reached. Pure inline impl in eval binary — no new public API, no production code change. **(2)** New eval case `onda_anaphoric_mid_sentence` — companion to `onda_must_not_be_ten_locative`. Same ambiguity, but онда appears MID-SENTENCE («Менің кітабым бар, онда суреттер көп.») — distinguishes "context unavailable" from "context available but unhelpful." **Results (n=19):** baseline 15/19 = 78.9%; all 5 prior strategies including with_context **17/19 = 89.5%**. `with_context` matches isolated-token strategies — **no additional lift**. Both онда cases (sentence-initial AND mid-sentence) still pick он. **Why context plumbing doesn't help:** both `он + Locative` and `ол + Locative` produce the SAME suffix chain (`noun:None|Singular|None|Locative|None`). Chain-level priors — unigram, bigram, smoothed, POS-conditioned — score these two analyses **identically**. Stable lex order picks он. The runtime layer doing context-aware re-ranking can't fix this; the signal needs to come from a different axis — **root-level priors** `P(root | suffix_chain)`, lexical co-occurrence, or genuine anaphor resolution at the dialog layer. This reshapes v4.20+ direction: next compositional ML layer is about adding root-identity to the prior axis, not deeper context plumbing in the FST. Pipeline: 1 binary extension (~50 lines) + 1 new eval case + 1 updated note. No production code changes. Workspace tests **807→807 passing**. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — measurement layer continues.** Next: v4.20.0+ (root-level priors to break the chain-collision tie), v4.20.5+ (corpus expansion + retraining).

**v4.19.0 — empirical eval of v4.15+ priors.** First minor in the v4.19+ measurement arc, long-deferred from v4.17.5. v4.15.0 → v4.17.0 shipped four prior strategies (unigram → bigram → smoothed → POS-conditioned) with anecdotal REPL evidence but no measured accuracy. v4.19.0 closes that loop. **Architectural addition:** `data/eval/parse_disambiguation_eval.json` — 20 hand-labeled cases of ambiguous Kazakh surface forms drawn from past live-REPL bugs (v3.9.5 неліктен → нелік, v4.3.5 онда → он, v4.4.10 қысқасы / ештеңе) plus cross-domain ambiguous content nouns (тіл, көз, шай, күй, тас, бар, кел, тау, шөл, ел, күн, көп, өз, қаза, алма, жоқ). Each case: surface, sentence context (for human review), gold root, note explaining the ambiguity. **New binary** `eval_parse_disambiguation` in `adam-corpus`: loads eval set + Lexicon + trained `SuffixPriors`, runs `analyse()` per token, applies five scoring strategies (baseline lexicographic / unigram v4.15.5 / bigram v4.16.0 / smoothed v4.16.5 α=0.3 / POS-conditioned v4.17.0), reports per-strategy accuracy + per-case detail (`=` / `⚠` markers). **Results (n=18 with non-empty FST parses):** baseline **15/18 = 83.3%**; all four prior strategies **17/18 = 94.4%** — **+11.1 pp lift from priors over the lexicographic baseline**. The four prior strategies collapse to identical scores on isolated tokens (no preceding chain → bigram/smoothed/POS-conditioned all fall back to unigram) — sanity check that higher-order tiers don't *regress* on no-context queries. Two cases where priors flip the wrong baseline pick: «неліктен» (baseline picks `нелік + Abl`, priors pick bare `неліктен`) and «алма» (baseline picks verb `ал`, priors pick noun `алма` = apple). One residual failure (all strategies): «онда» — gold = `ол + Loc` (anaphoric "there"), priors pick `он + Loc` ("in ten") — needs sentence context, beyond isolated-token scope. Two cases skipped (`қаза`, `өз`) — `analyse()` returns no parses; logged to stderr, removed from accuracy denominator. Pipeline: 1 new eval data file + 1 new binary + 1 `[[bin]]` registration. **No runtime code changes** — pure infrastructure / measurement. Workspace tests **806→807 passing**. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — measurement layer.** Next: v4.19.5+ (FST sentence-context plumbing for `онда`-class disambiguation), v4.20.0+ (corpus expansion + retraining priors over larger token base).

**v4.18.5 — composite-question handler + intro warmth template.** Patch in v4.18+ humanness arc closing two follow-up items deferred from v4.18.0. **(1)** New `SystemAspect::IntroAndCapabilities` + composite detector: requires identity-marker (`кім екен / сіз кімсіз / өзіңіз туралы`) + «және» + capabilities-marker (`не істей ала / мүмкіндіктер`), fires BEFORE individual aspect detectors. New template family `ask_about_system.intro_and_capabilities` surfaces both `system_kind` AND `system_capabilities` in sequence. Closes 2026-05-01 transcript turn 4 «Өзіңіз туралы, кім екеніңіз және не істей алатыныңыз туралы айтыңыз» where adam previously answered only the first half. **(2)** New `name_respect_distinct` slot — set ONLY when respect form differs from literal name (consonant-initial only). Auto-derived in `ensure_name_respect_slot` + `extract_slots(StatementOfName)`. New warm-intro template variant: «Танысқаныма қуаныштымын, {name}! Сізді {name_respect_distinct} деп атаймын — қазақ дәстүрі бойынша». Gated on `{name_respect_distinct}` so it auto-filters for vowel-initial names (Абай → name_respect = literal → no distinct form, no awkward «Сізді Абай деп атаймын»). For consonant-initial names (Дәулет/Марат/Серік) the user sees they were heard verbatim AND learns adam's address style with explicit cultural note. Pipeline: 1 new SystemAspect variant + 1 new template family + 1 new slot + 1 new template variant + composite detector. Workspace tests **806→806 passing** (+1 REPL replay regression dialog + 1 e2e test extended). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (5) — humanness through cultural fit — final patch.** Next: v4.19.0+ (empirical eval of v4.15+ priors, long-deferred from v4.17.5).

**v4.18.0 — respectful Kazakh address (Дәке/Мәке/Сәке) + list-class DialogContext tracking.** First minor in v4.18+. Two architectural additions explicitly directed by the user during v4.17.5 review. **(1) Respectful Kazakh address** — per Kazakh tradition a junior speaker addresses an older / honored person by «<first-consonant>әке» (Дәулет → Дәке, Марат → Мәке, Серік → Сәке). Adam is a young system addressing the human user — every post-introduction turn now uses the diminutive form. New `kazakh_respectful_address(name) -> Option<String>` helper in language_core (vowel-initial names like Абай return None, fall back to literal). New `is_kazakh_vowel(c)` covers all native Kazakh vowels. After `StatementOfName`, session stores BOTH `name` (literal) AND `name_respect` (diminutive). New `ensure_name_respect_slot` planner helper auto-derives respect form from name for direct-session-insert callers (tests/replay). 28 templates migrated to `{name_respect}`; 5 literal-name templates kept (first-ack warmth + `ask_name.with_known_user` recall). The split: first turn uses literal so user sees they were heard verbatim, subsequent turns use respect for warmth. **(2) List-class DialogContext tracking** — closes v4.17.5 known limitation. After each turn renders, `Conversation::turn_with_trace` stashes the rendered grounded_fact in session (cleared on no-grounded turns). `ToolContext` gains `previous_grounded_fact: Option<&'a str>`. `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` `list_intent_rank` extends with 4-tier fallback ladder: synonym query→object → synonym prev-fact→object → direct prev-fact-class→object → unmatched. Closes the «Оларды тізімдей аласыз ба?» case where adam previously surfaced rivers; now correctly surfaces the regions list because previous turn mentioned «облыс». 4 unit tests + 2 REPL replay regression dialogs. Workspace tests **802→806 passing**. **Stripe (5) — humanness through cultural fit — opens.** Next: v4.18.5 (composite-question handler «X жәнe Y» two-aspect splitter + intro warmth combining literal + respect: «Танысқаныма қуаныштымын, {name}! Сізді {name_respect} деп атаймын — қазақ дәстүрі бойынша.»), v4.19.0+ (empirical eval of v4.15+ priors).

**v4.17.5 — transcript-driven patch bundle (11 fixes from live REPL session).** Patch in the v4.x humanness arc. A 2026-05-01 live REPL session with the user surfaced 11 distinct issues across detection, mis-routing, and retrieval ranking. v4.17.5 closes all of them as a single coordinated bundle. **Detection misses (5):** (1) Creator-question detector + `тәрбиелеу` family — closes «А, сені кім тәрбиеледі?» which surfaced poetry pre-fix; (2) Birthdate + «дүниеге кел» — closes «қашан дүниеге келдіңіз?»; (3) SelfComparison + «ерекшелендіретін / айырмашылығыңыз»; (4) Capability-on-language combo + `қалай ... керектігін білесіз бе`; (5) NLM uppercase fix in intro template. **Mis-routing (3):** (6) list-anaphor gate — `аласыз ба` after list-verb + anaphor doesn't route to GenericCapability; plural anaphors `оларды/соларды/мұларды/бұларды + Acc/Dat/Gen` (12 forms) added to DISCOURSE_ANAPHORS; (7) Compliment tightened — defers when `бірақ + ма?/ба?` или `дайынсыз ба`; (8) New `Intent::AskWillingness` + detector + template family for «дайынсыз ба + verb-уге» pattern; (9) SelfComparison detector skips `жақсырақ болу / ақылды болу`. **Retrieval ranking (2):** (10) `list_intent_rank` reordered before overlap in SearchGraph cascade — synonym-aware sub-rank (`аймақ ↔ облыс`) so explicit «аймақтар тізімі» surfaces regions list, not landmarks; generic markers (`тізі / атау / барл`) excluded from direct overlap to prevent spurious matches; (11) New `geo_kz_115` rich Kazakhstan IsA («Орталық Азиядағы аумағы бойынша 9-шы үлкен тәуелсіз мемлекет; астанасы — Астана, ірі қаласы — Алматы») wins over bare «мемлекет» by length tier. Pipeline: 2 detector extensions + 1 helper + 1 new Intent + 1 new template family + 12 anaphor forms + 1 sort-cascade reorder + 1 world_core entry + `MULTIWORD_ENTITIES` += 1. **v4.17.0 — POS-conditioned priors P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain) + 4-tier fallback ladder.** Third minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.16.0 added bigrams, v4.16.5 added Jelinek-Mercer smoothing. v4.17.0 adds the **POS-aggregated fallback tier** — when a full bigram row is sparse but the previous token's POS is known, fall back to the POS-conditioned distribution before dropping to the unigram. Adds robustness for sparse contexts without exploding the artifact size (POS axis = 2 dimensions). **Architectural addition:** new field `SuffixPriors::pos_transition_log_prob: HashMap<String, HashMap<String, f32>>` keyed by POS string (`"noun"` / `"verb"`) → curr_chain → log_prob. Schema bumped 2→3. **(1)** `from_counts_with_bigrams` extended to compute POS-aggregated rows in parallel with full bigrams (zero extra training cost — same pass). **(2)** New helpers: `pos_from_chain_key(chain)` extracts POS prefix; `smooth_row(row)` extracted for code reuse. **(3)** Extended `score_chain_given_prev` 4-tier fallback ladder: **full bigram → POS-bigram → unigram → floor**. POS-bigram tier inserted when full-bigram row is empty OR sparse (curr unseen). Strictly additive: rich-context behaviour identical to v4.16.5. **(4)** SCHEMA_VERSION 2→3. **(5)** Training binary write_priors extracts `serialize_nested_map` helper used for both transition and POS-transition serialisation. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog. **Frozen artifact regenerated** at schema v3: 1112 chains, 21270 full bigrams across 711 prev rows, **846 POS-bigrams across 2 dense rows** (noun: 423 successors, verb: 423 successors). 1.4 MB JSON (POS adds ~16 KB — total artifact size effectively unchanged). Anti-regression 11/11 — POS-bigrams only fire on sparse-bigram-row paths, which canonical queries don't walk. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +1 field, score_chain_given_prev +1 fallback tier, training binary refactored. Workspace tests **799→802 passing** (+3 unit tests). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — fallback ladder layer.** Next: v4.17.5 (empirical eval — tiny held-out test set of FST-ambiguous tokens with hand-labelled correct readings, measure how often v4.16.0/v4.16.5/v4.17.0 each pick the labelled parse vs raw v3.2.0 lexicographic).

**v4.16.5 — Jelinek-Mercer interpolation knob α·log_p_unigram + (1-α)·log_p_bigram.** Patch in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.16.0 shipped pure bigram scoring with three-tier fallback. v4.16.5 adds the **smoothing dial**: a tunable interpolation weight between unigram and bigram log-probabilities. Lets the runtime balance the bigram's specificity (good when context is rich) against the unigram's robustness (good when bigram rows are sparse). **(1)** New `SuffixPriors::score_chain_smoothed(curr, prev, alpha)` + `score_noun_smoothed` + `score_verb_smoothed` — Jelinek-Mercer interpolation `α·log P(curr) + (1-α)·log P(curr|prev)`. `α` clamped to [0,1]. Symmetric early-outs for `α≈0` and `α≈1` keep the hot path fast. **(2)** New `Conversation::with_priors_alpha(α)` builder + `priors_alpha: Option<f32>` field. `None` preserves v4.16.0 pure-bigram-with-fallback path; `Some(α)` switches re-ranker to interpolation mode. **(3)** `parse_input_with_priors` signature extended with `alpha: Option<f32>`; all 4 call sites updated. Older callers passing only `priors` get bit-identical behaviour. **(4)** `adam_chat` defaults to `α = 0.3` (bigram-dominant with unigram smoothing). **Tunable via `ADAM_PRIORS_ALPHA` env var** for experimentation without recompilation. Startup line announces the chosen alpha. **(5)** 3 new unit tests (α=0 = pure bigram, α=1 = pure unigram, out-of-range clamps). **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog covers single-noun (minimal bigram) + multi-token (rich bigram) queries — both must answer correctly under smoothing. **Why α=0.3:** textbook Jelinek-Mercer for bigrams under Laplace-smoothed counts; bigram dominates (70%), unigram smooths sparse rows (30%). Empirically verified on 11-question anti-regression battery — v4.16.0 behaviour preserved on every canonical query while making prior more robust to unseen contexts. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +3 methods, Conversation +1 field +1 builder, parse_input chain extended with alpha, adam_chat startup attaches α=0.3 with env override. Workspace tests **796→799 passing** (+3 unit tests + 1 REPL replay). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — smoothing patch.** Next: v4.17.0 (POS-conditioned priors `P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain)` for sparse-mitigation).

**v4.16.0 — context-aware priors P(chain | preceding_chain) + greedy bigram-aware FST parse selection.** Second minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.15.0 shipped unigram priors `P(chain)`, v4.15.5 wired them into runtime parse selection. v4.16.0 extends to **context-aware bigrams** `P(chain | preceding_chain)` — captures local morphological agreement (e.g. Genitive followed by 3sg-Possessive — «жасушаның ядросы» — is much more probable than Genitive followed by Imperative). Same `корень + функция^n` compositional view, one Markov step deeper. **(1)** New `SuffixPriors::transition_log_prob: HashMap<String, HashMap<String, f32>>` field keyed by `(prev_chain, curr_chain)`. SCHEMA_VERSION bumped 1 → 2; v1 artifacts rejected by `load()`. **(2)** New `from_counts_with_bigrams` constructor with row-local add-one smoothing. **(3)** New `score_chain_given_prev` / `score_noun_given_prev` / `score_verb_given_prev` API with three-tier fallback ladder (no prev → unigram, unseen prev → unigram, unseen pair in known prev row → row floor). **(4)** Training binary updated with two-pass algorithm: first pass builds unique-token → chain-keys cache, second pass walks samples in order and tallies bigrams using the cache. Bigram pruning (count < 2.0) drops single-occurrence noise — 305K observed pairs → 21K retained, ~6× artifact size reduction. **(5)** Greedy bigram-aware parse selection in `parse_input_inner` — tracks the previous token's selected chain key, passes it into `score_chain_given_prev` when re-ranking candidates. Sentence starts / FST-empty tokens reset context. Stable sort preserves v3.2.0 lexicographic order on equal-prior parses. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog covers multi-token queries where bigram context matters. **Frozen artifact regenerated** as schema v2: 5,765,342 tokens, 1,112 chains, 305,856 bigrams observed → 21,270 retained, 711 transition rows; 1.4 MB JSON (was 70 KB unigram-only, well under 50 MB gitignore policy). 11-question anti-regression battery passes — bigram-aware re-rank doesn't disturb any v4.x behaviour. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +1 field + 1 constructor + 3 API methods, SCHEMA_VERSION bump, training-binary upgrade, runtime integration. Workspace tests **793→796 passing** (+3 unit tests + 1 schema-version assertion bumped). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — context-aware step.** Next: v4.16.5 (smoothing/interpolation knob α·log_p_unigram + (1-α)·log_p_bigram), v4.17.0 (POS-conditioned priors P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain)).

**v4.15.5 — SuffixPriors runtime integration: priors-aware FST parse selection.** Patch in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.15.0 shipped the trained `SuffixPriors` artifact + `load`/`score` API but explicitly deferred runtime integration to keep the architectural addition reversible. v4.15.5 wires the prior into the parse pipeline as a re-ranking signal: each turn's FST candidate analyses are now sorted by `P(chain)` DESC before downstream consumers see them. **Strictly additive** — when no priors are attached, the v3.2.0 deterministic lexicographic order is preserved bit-for-bit. **(1)** New `parse_input_with_priors` in lib.rs uses a stable comparator: parses scored higher by `P(chain)` move forward, ties retain the v3.2.0 lexicographic order. **(2)** `Conversation.suffix_priors: Option<SuffixPriors>` field + `with_suffix_priors(priors)` builder. **(3)** `Conversation::turn_with_trace` calls `parse_input_with_priors` with `self.suffix_priors.as_ref()`, threading the optional prior through the existing parse path. **(4)** `adam_chat` startup loads priors from `data/retrieval/suffix_chain_priors.json` (the v4.15.0 artifact), validates schema version, attaches via builder. Production startup now logs all four context layers: morpheme index, reasoning facts, domain index, **suffix priors (1112 chains over 5.77M training tokens)**. **(5)** Public exports tightened in adam-kernel-fst::lib. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog locks v4.x baseline behaviour through the priors pipeline. Pipeline: 1 new lib function + new Conversation field + new builder + adam_chat startup integration. Workspace tests **793→793 passing** (+1 REPL replay dialog). 13-question anti-regression battery passes — priors don't disturb any v4.x behaviour. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — first runtime patch.** Next: v4.16.0 (context-aware priors `P(chain | preceding_chain)` capturing local morphological agreement — one Markov step deeper, same compositional view).

**v4.15.0 — first compositional ML layer: P(suffix_chain) priors + offline training pass.** First minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. The Kazakh agglutinative grammar IS typed function composition (`root + suffix_1 + suffix_2 + ... + suffix_n`). Pre-v4.15.0 the FST analyser returned candidate parses in deterministic lexicographic order (v3.2.0 contract), but had no notion of which suffix-chains are actually *common* in Kazakh usage. v4.15.0 adds the missing distributional signal as a frozen, trained-offline prior over chain signatures, ready to inform downstream tie-breaking from v4.15.5 onward. Infrastructure-only release: the prior is loaded but not yet integrated into runtime decision-making — splitting the architectural addition from the behaviour change keeps both reversible. **Architectural addition:** new module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/suffix_priors.rs` (~280 lines + 8 tests). `struct SuffixPriors { version, trained_on_tokens, chain_log_prob }` — frozen lookup table from chain signature (e.g. `noun:None|Singular|None|Locative|None`) to natural-log probability. `SuffixPriors::load(path)` validates schema version (1 at v4.15.0). `SuffixPriors::from_counts` builds the prior with add-one (Laplace) smoothing. `score_noun` / `score_verb` are single hashmap probes. Unseen chains return `min_observed - ln(2)` so they rank strictly below the rarest observed chain. **Training pass:** new binary `crates/adam-corpus/src/bin/train_suffix_priors.rs`. Walks every `data/curated/*.json` pack, runs FST analyse on each token, attributes uniform `1/N` weight to each candidate parse (uniform attribution — unbiased given no labels), tallies counts, hands them to `SuffixPriors::from_counts`, writes `data/retrieval/suffix_chain_priors.json` as deterministic pretty-printed JSON (sorted keys for byte-stable output). **Why uniform attribution:** picking only the first parse would make the prior a circular reflection of the existing tie-breaker; uniform attribution captures which suffix chains *appear at all* in real Kazakh text. **Per the user's directive (`project_v4_direction`):** Predictable (pure frequency count, no embeddings/SGD), Cheap (5-min one-off training, single hashmap probe at runtime), Safe (only ranks pre-existing FST parses, never invents new ones), Foundation (preserves the `корень + функция^n` view, version-bump path is built in). Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 new binary + 1 frozen artifact + new dep edge `adam-corpus → adam-kernel-fst`. Workspace tests **785→793 passing** (+8). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) — compositional ML — opens.** Next: v4.15.5 (runtime integration in `best_noun_hint` as tiebreaker), v4.16.0 (context-aware priors `P(chain | preceding_chain)`).

**v4.14.5 — predicate decomposition wiring + domain-aware retrieval reranker.** Patch in the v4.12+ humanness arc. v4.13.0 introduced `sentence_decomp` (case-role decomposition) and v4.14.0 introduced `DomainIndex` + `DialogContext.current_domain`. v4.14.5 wires both into the runtime path so they actually influence behavior — strictly additive, no regression risk. **(1)** Domain-aware retrieval tiebreaker — `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` sort cascade gains a new tier between `user_facing_fact_priority` and `raw_text length`: when both `current_domain` AND `domain_index` are attached, candidates whose subject's primary domain matches the currently-discussed domain win over equal-priority candidates from other domains. Useful for cross-domain ambiguous topics (`тіл` linguistics OR biology body part, `көз` biology OR geography spring, `сай` botany OR geography). Strictly additive — only fires on ties. **(2)** `ToolContext` extended with `current_domain: Option<&'a str>` + `domain_index: Option<&'a DomainIndex>`. Both `Some` only when v4.14.0+ wiring is attached; older callers pass `None`/empty index, preserving pre-v4.14.5 behaviour bit-for-bit. **(3)** `Conversation::turn_with_trace` wires new fields. Empty-index short-circuit means tiebreaker doesn't even run when index has nothing to say. **(4)** `sentence_decomp` focus fallback in `interpret_text_with_lexicon` — when greedy `best_noun_hint` returns None, `sentence_decomp::decompose` runs; if its `focus` is set AND `focus_role ∈ {Subject, Object, Source, Locus}`, it becomes the noun_hint. Strictly additive. Predicate-role focus excluded so a bare verb root is never promoted as topic. **(5)** NOT_A_TOPIC re-check on the fallback path — fixed an early v4.14.5 regression where sentence_decomp fallback bypassed v4.4.10 closed-class additions (`қысқа`, `ештеңе`, etc) because sentence_decomp keeps its own smaller list. The re-check applies the full `NOT_A_TOPIC` filter, restoring `qysqasy_does_not_get_extracted_as_topic`. **(6)** 2 new REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: ToolContext +2 fields + new domain-match tiebreaker tier + new fallback path; workspace tests **785→785 passing** (+2 REPL replay dialogs). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (3) — domain awareness — final patch closes the architectural-wiring gap.** Next: v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer: `P(suffix_chain)` priors).

**v4.14.0 — DomainIndex foundation + DialogContext.current_domain wiring + curriculum-content honest fallback.** Third minor in the v4.12+ humanness arc. v4.13.0 introduced `DialogContext` with `current_domain` slot but left it always `None` (no topic→domain mapping). v4.14.0 builds the missing index, wires it through `Conversation`, and adds the third 2026-05-01 transcript failure handler. **Architectural addition:** new module `crates/adam-dialog/src/domain_index.rs` (~150 lines): `DomainIndex { by_topic: HashMap<String, String> }` — topic root → primary World-Core domain. `DomainIndex::build(entries)` walks every fact, tallies (root, domain) counts; primary = majority winner with alphabetical tie-break for full determinism. `DomainIndex::lookup_domain(topic)` is case-insensitive O(1). Built once at `adam_chat` startup from `data/world_core/*.jsonl` — **1 644 topics indexed across 38 domains**. **(1)** New `Conversation::with_domain_index(idx)` builder + per-turn `DialogContext.current_domain` population via `domain_index.lookup_domain(noun_hint)`. The existing v4.13.0 majority-vote logic (`recompute_domain` over the last DOMAIN_WINDOW=4 turns) settles `current_domain` on the currently-discussed subject area. **(2)** `adam_chat` startup integration — loads world_core via `adam_reasoning::world_core::load_world_core_dir`, builds index, attaches via builder. Failure to load is non-fatal (empty index, no-ops cleanly). **(3)** New `Intent::AskCurriculumContent` variant + detector + template family `ask_curriculum_content`. Pattern: subject (student-class: `оқушы / студент / шәкірт`) + education locus (`мектеп / сабақ / сыныпта / университет / колледж`) + question word `не` + learning verb (`оқиды / үйренеді / оқисың / оқисыз / ...`). Conservative — requires ALL four signals so generic «оқушы туралы не білесіз?» doesn't accidentally route here. Catches «Оқушылар мектепте физика пәнінен не оқиды?» and «Студенттер университетте не оқиды?». Pre-v4.14.0 surfaced greedy IsA fact about `оқушы`. Honest fallback: «Бұл сұрағыңыз оқу бағдарламасының мазмұнына қатысты — менде нақты пәндік дерек жоқ. Мен әр пәннің не екенін, негізгі ұғымдары мен маңызды атауларын айтып бере аламын». **(4)** New `IntentKind::AskCurriculumContent` companion variant. **(5)** 2 new REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: 1 new module + new Conversation field + new Intent variant + new template family + DomainIndex now actually populated (was always None pre-v4.14.0); workspace tests **777→785 passing** (+8 domain_index unit tests). **All three 2026-05-01 transcript failures now closed across v4.13.0/v4.13.5/v4.14.0.** Stripe (3) — domain awareness — opens. Next: v4.14.5 (predicate decomposition wiring + domain-aware retrieval reranker), v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer: `P(suffix_chain)` priors).

**v4.13.5 — capability honest fallbacks: generic verb-capability + multi-topic capability detection.** Patch in the v4.12+ humanness arc. v4.13.0 laid the foundation (sentence_decomp + DialogContext + closed-class hygiene) and intentionally deferred the answer-side work; v4.13.5 closes the two known gaps explicitly listed in the v4.13.0 release notes by adding two new `SystemAspect` variants. **(1)** `SystemAspect::GenericCapability` + detector for `<verb-converb> ала<person> <ма/ба/па>?` pattern — surface forms `аласың/аласыз ба/ма`, `ала ма?`, `алады ма`. Distinct from `Capabilities` (v4.6.0 — language-only with closed adverb prefix) and `Limitations` (v4.6.0 — `алмайсың/алмайсыз`). Catches «Сіз бағдарлама жаза аласыз ба?», «Сіз есептей аласыз ба?», «Сіз оны бағдарламалай аласыз ба?» (now resolves `оны → Rust` via v4.13.0 DialogContext, then routes to GenericCapability). **(2)** `SystemAspect::MultiTopicCapability` + detector for 2+ commas (counted on raw input — `joined` strips punctuation) + `және` + `білесің/білесіз`. Catches «Сіз математика, физика, химия... білесіз бе?». Pre-v4.13.5 surfaced `Мектеп — білім беру мекемесі`. **(3)** `detect_ask_about_system` signature extended with `raw_input: &str` so punctuation-sensitive detectors (comma-count) can run. **(4)** Two new fields on `SystemIdentity` (`generic_capability_summary` ~80 words + `multi_topic_capability_summary` ~50 words) + 2 new template families. **All three 2026-05-01 transcript failures now closed.** Pipeline: 2 new SystemAspect variants + 2 new SystemIdentity fields + 2 new template families + 11 new surface-form patterns. Workspace tests: 777 → **777 passing** (+2 REPL replay dialogs). Cadence: patch (v4.13.5). **Stripe (2) — humanness — final patch.** Next: v4.14.0 (predicate decomposition + domain-TF-IDF + semantic-cohesion graph traversal), v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer: `P(suffix_chain)` priors).

**v4.13.0 — sentence-decomposition foundation + DialogContext multi-turn topic memory + closed-class hygiene.** Second minor in the v4.12+ humanness arc. The 2026-05-01 live-REPL transcript surfaced two systemic gaps: (a) **greedy first-noun-match** — modal particles / negators (`әлі / әлде / мүмкін / тағы / жоқ / иә / па / пе`) leaked into noun_hint as if they were content nouns, surfacing poetry; (b) **goldfish memory** — only one back-reference (`session["last_query_topic"]`) was tracked, so a turn referring to a topic from 3-4 turns earlier could not be resolved. v4.13.0 lays foundation for both. **Architectural addition #1** — new module `crates/adam-dialog/src/sentence_decomp.rs` (~470 lines): the Kazakh agglutinative grammar IS typed function composition (`root + suffix-chain` where each case suffix is `Noun → CaseMarkedNoun[Role]`); FST already decomposes this, downstream code finally USES it. `enum SentenceType { Question, Statement, Imperative, Exclamation }` + `enum Role` (11 variants: Subject/Object/Locus/Source/Recipient/Possessor/Instrument/Predicate/QuestionWord/Closed/Coord) + `struct SentenceDecomposition { sentence_type, tokens, question_word, focus, focus_role, predicate, topic_list, cohesion }` + `fn decompose(input, parses, last_topic)` — pure function, O(n) over tokens, hardmap lookups only, microseconds per query. Question-word focus override: `не` asks for OBJECT, `қайда` LOCUS, `қашан/қалай/неліктен` PREDICATE, `кім/қандай` SUBJECT. **Architectural addition #2** — new module `crates/adam-dialog/src/dialog_context.rs` (~250 lines): `DialogContext { topic_history: Vec<TopicMention>, last_topic, subject_under_discussion, current_domain }` with capped FIFO history (MAX_HISTORY=64), majority-vote subject inference over STICKY_WINDOW=6 turns (one-off mentions don't displace), majority-vote domain over DOMAIN_WINDOW=4 turns. `resolve_anaphor()` consults `subject_under_discussion` first, falls back to `last_topic`. New `Conversation.dialog_context` field, updated each turn after Intent::Unknown.noun_hint resolves. **(1)** Closed-class additions to `NOT_A_TOPIC`: 8 entries (`әлі / әлде / мүмкін / тағы / жоқ / иә / па / пе` — modal/discourse particles + existential negator + post-voiceless allomorphs of question particle, completing the `ма/ме/ба/бе/па/пе` paradigm). **(2)** Acc/Dat/Gen anaphor extension to `DISCOURSE_ANAPHORS`: 12 forms (`оны/соны/мұны/бұны/оған/соған/мұған/бұған/оның/соның/мұның/бұның`) — pre-v4.13.0 only Loc + Abl cases were registered, so «Сіз оны бағдарламалай аласыз ба?» («оны» = "it" Acc) was ignored. **(3)** Multi-turn anaphora live-test: turn 1 «Rust туралы білесіз бе?» establishes Rust as topic; turn 2 «Сіз оны...» now resolves «оны → Rust» via DialogContext. **(4)** 2 new REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: 2 new modules + new `Conversation` field + 12 closed-class entries + 12 anaphor forms; workspace tests **758→777 passing** (+19: 11 sentence_decomp unit tests + 8 dialog_context unit tests). **Zero ML.** Probabilistic suffix-chain prior (`P(suffix_chain)` — natural `root + function^n` learning) reserved for v4.15+. Next: v4.13.5 (generic capability detector + honest fallback templates), v4.14.0 (predicate decomposition + domain-TF-IDF), v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer).

**v4.12.0 — humanness milestone: question-shape classifier + Implementation aspect + causal-reasoning routing + backtick carve-out for user output.** First minor in the v4.12+ humanness research arc. Stripe (1) — "answer-by-the-point" — closed across all 38 world_core domains in v4.11.5/.6/.7; v4.12.0 opens stripe (2) — "human-like reasoning" — by giving the planner an analytical signal it never had: the **form** of the user's question (definition vs causal vs listing vs comparison vs yes/no), independent of topic. **Architectural addition:** new `crates/adam-dialog/src/question_shape.rs` module with `QuestionShape` enum (5 variants: Definition, Causal, YesNoCheck, Listing, Comparison) + pure surface-level `detect(input) -> Option<QuestionShape>`; new `Intent::Unknown.question_shape: Option<QuestionShape>` field populated at the top of `interpret_text_with_lexicon`; preserved across `verifier::strip_evidence`. **(1)** New `SystemAspect::Implementation` variant + detector for «Сіз қандай тілде жазылғансыз?» / «Не тілінде жасалғансың?» / «Қандай бағдарламалау тілінде жазылған?» + template family `ask_about_system.implementation` rendering new `SystemIdentity::implementation_summary` (mentions `Rust`, the crate stack `adam-kernel/tokenizer/dialog/reasoning/retrieval/corpus`, FST + rule-based architecture, `macOS`/`Linux` platform support). Closes the v4.11.7 known gap. **(2)** Causal-reasoning routing — when `Intent::Unknown` carries `QuestionShape::Causal`, the planner short-circuits to `unknown.causal.with_fact` (grounded_fact present) or `unknown.causal.bare` (noun-only). Honest hedging: adam states what it knows about X, then explicitly says it cannot pinpoint the cause from its dataset. Closes «Неліктен жасуша өледі?» which pre-v4.12.0 surfaced a generic IsA fact (logically wrong: adam asserted "X IS Y" when the user asked "WHY does X happen?"). **(3)** Backtick carve-out in `audit_response::contains_latin` — mirrors v4.7.0 corpus-purity carve-out, now applied to user-facing output. Backtick-quoted spans bypass `LatinCharactersForbidden` so technical proper nouns (`Rust`, `Cargo`, `String`, `macOS`, `Linux`, `adam-kernel`) appear verbatim; bare Latin prose outside backticks still trips the gate. **(4)** 5 new REPL replay regression dialogs (Implementation × 2 + Causal × 2 + carryover). Pipeline: 3 new template families (`ask_about_system.implementation`, `unknown.causal.with_fact`, `unknown.causal.bare`); workspace tests **749→758 passing** (+9 new: 6 question_shape + 3 backtick-audit); world_core 1 625/1 791/38 unchanged. Both v4.11.7-known gaps now answer correctly. Stripe (2) opens; v4.12.5 = discourse-acknowledgement + template rotation; v4.13.0 = graph-cohesion answer composition.

**v4.11.5 — humanlike-dialog patch bundle: 5 fixes from live REPL transcript review.** First release in the v4.12+ "human-like dialog" research arc per `project_humanlike_dialog_directive`. All 5 are catastrophic correctness failures from the 2026-04-30 transcript: «Адам, сен мектептің физика бағдарламасын білесің бе?» pre-v4.11.5 returned `адам IsA сүтқоректі`; «Rust туралы не білесіз?» returned a poetry quote about the body part `тіл`. **(1)** Vocative-addressee guard (`discourse::strip_addressee`) strips leading `Адам, …` / `Адам! …` / `Адам сен …` BEFORE FST parsing, disambiguated from definitional `Адам — сүтқоректі.` by an addressee signal in the input. **(2)** World_core source-priority in topic extraction — `multiword_entity_hint` promoted to run BEFORE `topic_marker_hint` in `best_noun_hint`; plus inflected-form lemma fallback in `topic_marker_hint` that walks parses to find the longest noun-root which is a prefix of the inflected surface form, closing the v4.11.0 `Тілі` fake-proper-noun bug. **(3)** Curriculum compounds in MULTIWORD_ENTITIES (+9 query-time): `физика бағдарламасы`, `химия бағдарламасы`, `биология бағдарламасы`, `мектеп пәндері`, etc. **(4)** New `adam_self.jsonl` world_core domain (27 entries / 27 facts) with identity (`adam IsA тілдік модель / диалог жүйесі / когнитивтік ядро`), implementation (`adam related_to rust`, `adam IsA ретривал жүйесі`), per-domain knowledge claims (`adam has физика білімі / химия білімі / …`), and curriculum-program facts (`физика бағдарламасы IsA мектеп пәні` …). 21 new compounds added to MULTIWORD_ENTITIES. `SystemIdentity::knowledge_summary` refreshed to enumerate all 38 domains. **(5)** Latin-name passthrough (`semantics::latin_subject_hint`) closes the v4.7.0 known limitation — closed list of 47 Latin-named technical subjects; when the user types one as a Latin word (case-insensitive, word-boundary-matched), it becomes the topic, so «Rust туралы не білесіз?» grounds on `\`Rust\` — жадыны қауіпсіз басқаратын жүйелік бағдарламалау тілі` instead of poetry. All 5 transcript questions land on the correct world_core fact post-v4.11.5.

**v4.11.0 milestone — `history_kazakhstan.jsonl` world_core domain (history of Kazakhstan, Kazakh).** Ninth v4.x minor; **final** in the non-Rust domain expansion track. **v4.7.20 milestone — Rust Book Chapter 20 (Соңғы жоба: көп ағынды веб-сервер) translated, in pack — TRANSLATION SERIES COMPLETE.** Twentieth and final chapter under «глава = патч» cadence. Full Kazakh translation of Rust Book Chapter 20 — Final Project: Building a Multithreaded Web Server — the capstone chapter that ties together everything from chapters 1–19 into one real working program: a multithreaded HTTP server with graceful shutdown. Sections: building a single-threaded web server (`TcpListener`, HTTP request structure, response writing, serving HTML, request validation with `/` and `/sleep` and 404 paths); turning it multithreaded with a `ThreadPool` (compiler-driven development workflow, `mpsc::channel` + `Arc<Mutex<Receiver>>` for sharing the channel across workers, `Worker` struct with id and `JoinHandle`, the `Job = Box<dyn FnOnce() + Send + 'static>` type alias); graceful shutdown via `Drop` on `ThreadPool` (closing the channel by dropping the `sender`, joining all worker threads, the `Option::take` pattern). New `data/raw/rust_book_kk/chapter_20.md` (~5 500 words). **Translation series totals:** 20 chapters, ~95 000 Kazakh words, 1 543 sentence-level samples in `data/curated/rust_book_kk_pack.json`, all licensed MIT/Apache-2.0 with original attribution. Pack: 19 chapters / 1 459 samples → **20 chapters / 1 543 samples**. Morpheme index unchanged (rust_book pack still at 500-per-pack ceiling — switching to `--full` mode is the next architectural step). Workspace 745 unchanged. The Rust Book translation thread is now closed.

**v4.7.19 follow-up — Rust Book Chapter 19 (Жетілдірілген мүмкіндіктер) translated, in pack («глава = патч» cadence; the broadest chapter of the book).** Full Kazakh translation surveying five advanced topic areas: `unsafe` Rust (the five superpowers — raw pointer deref, `unsafe fn`, `static mut`, `unsafe impl`, `union`; FFI via `extern "C"` and `#[no_mangle]`; building safe abstractions over unsafe with the `split_at_mut` example); advanced traits (associated types vs generics, default generic parameters with `Add<Rhs = Self>`, fully-qualified syntax `<Type as Trait>::method`, supertraits, the newtype pattern for the orphan-rule workaround); advanced types (newtype for type-safety wrappers, `type` aliases, the never type `!`, dynamically-sized types and `?Sized`); advanced functions and closures (function pointers `fn(T) -> U` vs `Fn` traits, returning closures via `Box<dyn Fn>` or `impl Fn`); macros (declarative `macro_rules!` with the `vec!` walkthrough, procedural macros split into derive / attribute / function-like, the `proc-macro` crate convention with `syn` + `quote`). New `data/raw/rust_book_kk/chapter_19.md` (~6 500 words). Chapter-19-specific terminology: raw pointer → **шикі көрсеткіш**, FFI → **шетел функцияларының интерфейсі**, union → **одақ**, associated type → **байланысты тип**, supertrait → **ата-трейт**, newtype pattern → **жаңатип үлгісі**, type alias → **тип бүркеншегі**, never type → **ешқашан-тип `!`**, dynamically-sized type → **динамикалық өлшемді тип**, function pointer → **функция көрсеткіші**, declarative macro → **декларативті макрос**, procedural macro → **процедуралық макрос**.
